# **229 – The Witch's Relic**

Simultaneously with the Abyss Serpent’s collapse, the compressed water was released. A massive amount of water swallowed the lower part of the great hall like a tsunami, rapidly raising the water level.

Alvelinde’s form was—embedded and stuck in the shattered wall. The area where the serpent’s fangs had bitten into her had a gaping hole torn through it, and the rest of her body appeared to have suffered fatal damage from the water pressure and current.

As I approached with Ouroboros still in stance, Alvelinde closed her eyes and smiled.

“It was an enjoyable fight, but in this state, I cannot continue. He told me to avoid engaging the Demon Slayer… Indeed, he was right. Kuku…”

By “he,” she probably meant… not the Crown Prince of Silvatoria. Gardinis had also mentioned it—it makes more sense to think of him as the leader among the demons.

If that’s the case, then she likely had objectives as part of the demon group separate from the Crown Prince’s goals. Given that she came at the time of the seal’s release, perhaps she aimed to transport the Miasma Orb or, if possible, steal the Orb. Whether the Crown Prince knew about this or not is another matter.

“Did you bring the Miasma Orb with you?”

“…If you’ve already figured that out, this will be quick. If you want it, you can search through my belongings at the inn.”

…Just as I thought. Since the Miasma Orb is related to the seal, it’s problematic that we can’t simply destroy it recklessly. Nor can we just abandon its management. We’ll have to continue investigating the Miasma Orb.

“Still… I never imagined an exception like you would exist—Ah. So that’s what it means to be able to use Circulation. Patricia, was it? You too… carry the blood of those sorcerers.”

When my eyes widened, Alvelinde laughed cheerfully.

“What do you know?”

“Who can say? If you pursue the answers, you’ll likely find out eventually. After all, you’re probably the greatest obstacle to our plans.”

Alvelinde’s limbs began dissolving into particles of light from their ends, vanishing into the Magic Light Water Vein.

“It seems my time has come. It’s been a while… but I enjoyed it. I’m satisfied.”

With those final words, her eyes closed while maintaining a smile, Alvelinde scattered into the void.

I took a deep breath and shook my head. A stinging pain spread throughout my body.

While I had burns here and there and numerous small cuts… well, it was within acceptable limits. I gently patted the heads of Ouroboros, who was making worried sounds, along with Nemea and Capella to reassure them.

The method of wrapping the portion of Internal Magic Power I couldn’t contain internally around my body for control didn’t feel particularly burdensome either. Of course, this time I didn’t use my own body as a medium to cast magic, so it’s not a direct comparison.

Have I become stronger than before? And can I become even stronger going forward? I want to believe I’m moving forward. Strong enough to crush whatever schemes they’re plotting with the Miasma Orb and keep advancing.

“Theodore-sama!”

Led by Ashley, everyone came rushing over.

“I managed to finish it.”

“Please let me see your injuries.”

Ashley’s expression looked like she might burst into tears at any moment. Wanting to reassure her, I smiled back and began removing my jacket.

The glow of Healing Magic lit at Ashley’s fingertips as she treated the small cuts on my cheeks and shoulders, along with the burned areas on my arms, chest, back, and waist. When Ashley’s slender fingers touched me, the pain subsided. It had been a while since I received treatment for burns.

Healing Shell for burns was applied to me. The cool sensation felt pleasant.

Not just Ashley, but everyone wore similarly worried expressions.

Yeah. I feel like I’m always making them worry. That’s right. It would be best if I could win more easily. I really need to become stronger.

“I’ll become stronger. So you won’t have to worry.”

When I said that, Ashley gently leaned against me from behind and continued the treatment.

“—Finished. But please don’t push yourself too hard.”

Saying this, Ashley, who had moved away, showed a slightly troubled smile.

“Thank you, Ashley.”

“Yes.”

Ashley placed a hand on her chest and nodded slightly.

“What about everyone else’s injuries?”

“Regarding injuries, we’re fine this time.”

“Is that… so? That’s good.”

When I stroked Ashley’s hair, she smiled bashfully. First, I need to eliminate the recoil and perform Circulating Ki, which will also serve as rest and recovery. Since the footing is shallow water, I used Earth Magic to create a smooth stone platform.

I applied a Seal to Grace and embraced her along with Ashley. When I wrapped my arms around their shoulders to eliminate the recoil, they smiled back and buried their faces in my chest.

Hmm… Last time, Virginia, who Grace dealt with, was a vampire… and in many ways, she was someone who matched well with Grace. Compared to before, the recoil feels relatively mild this time.

When I embraced Marlene, she wrapped her arms around my waist and clung tightly. I stroked Marlene’s hair as she looked at me with a smile.

“Claudia.”

“Yes.”

Though her cheeks reddened slightly, she smiled and leaned against me somewhat hesitantly. I then activated Circulating Ki. Perhaps because teleportation was a major technique for Claudia too, she seemed to have consumed quite a bit of Magical Power. Performing Circulating Ki with multiple people like this creates synergistic effects. Each person’s fatigue decreases, and recovery speeds up.

Body warmth and soft sensations. Gentle fragrances that filled my nostrils. I gathered and elevated the flow of everyone’s Magical Power.

“…It’s warm.”

Grace’s quiet voice. Marlene nodded slightly. We continued like that, surrendering to the surge of Magical Power, performing Circulating Ki for a while before separating.

“Marie… are you okay?”

After all, Rosemary’s connection enhancement with her Doll was also quite a major technique.

“If you mean Magical Power consumption, it’s not that bad. I’ve already recovered quite a bit.”

She says that, but… hmm. It would probably be good to perform Circulating Ki with Rosemary too.

“Marie, come over here too.”

“Um. Circulating Ki… I suppose?”

“Yeah. Magical Power depletion can affect your physical condition later.”

“…Still. Being the only one is a bit…”

Rosemary seemed somewhat hesitant.

“In that case, how about doing it like we did at the lake?”

“Ah. Us too?”

“Yes. And we don’t need to hug like we did at the lake.”

Sheila and Irmhild said. Seraphina immediately perched happily on my shoulder. That seemed to satisfy Rosemary. She hid her mouth with her feather fan and sat down beside me.

Sheila took my right hand. Rosemary took my left hand.

“Um. Then would it be alright if I used my tail?”

“Anywhere you’re touching is fine.”

Irmhild said somewhat hesitantly as she wrapped her tail around my side. It had a smooth texture and feel…. Hmm. Then let’s begin Circulating Ki.

“…Really. It’s warm.”

“The fatigue doesn’t linger afterward.”

Irmhild responded to Rosemary’s murmured words. Since she seemed tired from the theater performance, I’d been performing Circulating Ki with Irmhild too.

We continued Circulating Ki like that for a while, and just as we finished, a communication came through on the Communication Device.

‘Lady Tephra’s Curse has disappeared. We have confirmed that the Curse on Marquis Zilbolt’s wife and daughter has also vanished.’

It was from Mercedes of the Knight Order. Probably because Alvelinde had been destroyed.

Caduceus had already notified them that the opponent was a Demon and had been defeated.

“Ah—It seems we need to recover the Miasma Orb. Apparently, the Demon brought it to the inn.”

I’ve caught my breath, so let’s get moving. That falls under my jurisdiction. I can’t leave it to others, nor can we just leave it as is.

“You’re safe. When I heard the report that it was a Demon, I was worried about your safety.”

Just as Alvelinde had said.

After recovering the Miasma Orb and heading to the Royal Castle, King Melvin in battle attire was the first to come running.

“The outcome is as you see. We sustained some minor injuries on our side, but as you can see, that’s the extent of it.”

When I showed him the Healing Shell, King Melvin closed his eyes.

“…You have truly done a great service.”

I handed the sphere emitting Miasma to the Mage Corps. The Mage Corps members wore tense expressions as two of them used Levitation to carry it away.

“Hmm. What about this luggage?”

“These are the Witch’s belongings. There are several points that concern me.”

“This is…”

When I showed him what I’d found, King Melvin’s expression darkened.

The scene at the central district inn was still in Confusion, but just as Alvelinde had said, we were able to discover the Miasma Orb among her luggage. That much went according to plan.

The other items were mostly… clothing, travel funds, passes, and other travel preparations. Among Alvelinde’s belongings, what caught my attention were what appeared to be catalysts made from processed Transference Stones, and passes issued by Silvatoria.

Though Alvelinde herself had vanished… these were physical evidence showing her connection with public figures from Silvatoria. They would serve as effective countermeasures against the Crown Prince.

“Passes and catalysts. Indeed, these are concerning… but for today, I will handle the cleanup, so please rest slowly and recover your energy. I will contact you with any findings about the Witch’s possessions.”

“Thank you.”

This time—compared to when we faced Gardinis, the injuries were lighter, but I had gone all out, darting around and firing High-Tier Magic with dual internal and external Magical Power, so I’d done quite a bit. If I can rest like this, nothing would be better.

“And also—we’ve received requests from Spirit Tephra and Marquis Zilbolt wishing to meet with you… but I told them to make it tomorrow or later. You all must be tired from today as well.”

Seeing off King Melvin’s wry smile, I left the Royal Castle.

I’ll have to go meet with Tephra and Marquis Zilbolt tomorrow or so.

+++

# **230 – The Blessing of Tephra**

“Good day.”

“Ambassador, this way.”

When I appeared at the ritual site with everyone by carriage, the shrine maidens of the Moon Temple quietly bowed to welcome us.

Not only Tephra but Marquis Zilbolt should also be at the ritual site. After being sent here via Teleportation Magic, they had been under the protection of the Knight Order and Mage Corps.

Since Tephra wanted to speak with me, the Marquis apparently decided not to relocate elsewhere and waited for my visit instead.

“Well then, I’ll go speak with the two of them for a bit.”

“Yes.”

Grace and the others would wait at the lodging facilities during our conversation. Since Penelope was there too, Marlene looked delighted.

Hearing they were at the gazebo, I headed that way to find Tephra speaking with Marquis Zilbolt and his wife and daughter. The relationship between Tephra and the Marquis was probably similar to that between Claudia and King Melvin. Marquis Zilbolt appeared quite reverent toward Tephra.

“Oh, Theodore!”

“Ambassador, sir.”

Noticing my presence, Tephra’s face broke into a smile, while Marquis Zilbolt and his family stood and bowed deeply.

“I see everyone is gathered.”

“We’ve all been waiting for you. I wished to thank you for splendidly keeping your promise to me. As you can see, the Curse has completely vanished.”

Tephra slightly opened the collar of her flame-like robe and smiled.

“That’s good to hear. If the Curse Magic hadn’t disappeared just by defeating the Witch, we would have needed to head to Mt. Tephra.”

“Personally, I thought traveling with you all wouldn’t have been so bad either.”

Tephra gave a wry smile before continuing.

“Of course, the Curse has vanished from these two as well. I have matters to discuss with you too… but yes. It seems this fellow has something he wishes to tell you. Perhaps we should start with that?”

“I don’t mind that,” I replied, and Marquis Zilbolt nodded before speaking.

“First, allow me to express my gratitude. For saving not only my subjects but also the lives of my wife and daughter. How could I possibly repay such a debt?… No, before that, I must apologize for causing disturbances around you, Ambassador, and within the Kingdom of Verdugal, and accept the consequences for that.”

“I’m just glad you’re safe. I’ve duly received your words of thanks and apology.”

Consequences, huh. But I’m not in a position to decide that, and in terms of personal defense, the objective has been achieved. So that would likely be King Melvin’s or the King of Silvatoria’s responsibility. Even then, given the circumstances…

King Melvin was proactive about rescuing Marquis Zilbolt, so I doubt he’d make unreasonable demands.

Well… From Marquis Zilbolt’s perspective, he probably feels he owes an unrepayable debt to me and the Kingdom of Verdugal.

“I’m not in a position to demand consequences or punishment from you, Marquis. I simply hope this incident leads to friendship between our two nations and peace for the people.”

The Marquis closed his eyes at my words and bowed deeply once more. That’s about all I have to say to the Marquis. If I can obtain information about Silvatoria’s domestic affairs from him, that would suffice for me.

Regarding Silvatoria matters—it would probably be best to include King Melvin.

As the conversation with Marquis Zilbolt reached a natural pause, Tephra turned to face me directly.

“Now then, Theodore. I have something I wish to give you.”

“What might that be?”

“You kept your promise to me, even while bearing such injuries.”

Tephra glanced at the Healing Shell applied to my burns before meeting my gaze straight on.

“As your ally, I cannot remain silent without giving you something in return. I bestow my Blessing upon you and those close to you. And to this ritual site you created for me, I wish to leave a token of our friendship.”

“Lady Tephra’s Blessing…?”

The Marquis’s eyes widened.

“Indeed. You shall gain Resistance to fire and cold. Minor incidents will no longer cause burns, and even in blizzards you shall not lose your warmth. However… you remain human. Please understand that my Blessing is not absolute.”

…Well, even if it’s not absolute, Resistance to fire and ice is pretty valuable. Being a volcano Spirit, she probably has affinity with fire, and regarding ice, it might relate to providing warmth through hot springs. Moreover, from her tone, it seems the effect will extend to all Party Members.

“That would—be very helpful,” I replied, and Tephra narrowed her eyes happily.

“And regarding the token of friendship I leave at this ritual site… I believe I can make hot water spring from the land, similar to near the mountain.”

Near Mt. Tephra—meaning like the Marquis’s territory, having hot water spring forth…

“Um. Does that mean hot springs will emerge?”

“Indeed. There was a pond in the garden you created, correct? I wish to make hot water spring from there.”

“Would that be the same hot springs as in my territory?” the Marquis asked.

“That should be the case.”

Marquis Zilbolt nodded at Tephra’s words.

“Ambassador, though it may sound like hometown pride, those hot springs are truly wonderful. They warm you to the core, and are said to have medicinal properties when consumed as well.”

“So they can be used for therapeutic baths?”

“Yes. They’re said to make skin glossy, smooth, and radiant.”

Marquis Zilbolt nodded.

Hot springs sound appealing. Even more so if they have medicinal properties. I’d been considering how to utilize the ritual site—this might just be perfect.

“However, there is one problem with implementing this. There is some kind of—even to my eyes, mysterious power at work in this land. If I could speak with whoever governs this place and obtain their consent, I believe my power could reach here…”

“In that case, I can probably introduce you.”

“Oh ho! As expected of my ally.”

Tephra laughed delightedly at my response, while Marquis Zilbolt blinked in surprise.

“To conclude, it’s possible,” Claudia stated simply when I brought Tephra to her and asked if it could be done.

“Is that so?”

“It’s different from trying to alter the Labyrinth’s core. Like the mine’s labyrinthification too… it moves surprisingly easily in expansion directions.”

Altering the Labyrinth’s core. Meaning since Claudia, as the administrator, is necessary for the Labyrinth’s maintenance, the Labyrinth will defend itself even against her will. That defense takes the form of Monsters or Guardians prone to Rampage… These malfunctions conflict with the goal of strengthening the people living around the Labyrinth, creating complications.

“Probably, just forming a contract between Tephra and me will allow the Labyrinth to support it using Tephra’s power as the core. If we consider therapeutic baths as maintaining people’s health, it aligns with the direction I’ve aimed for from the start.”

According to Claudia, while more advanced Magic Formulas were used for the Spirit Hall and Moonlight Temple deep in the Labyrinth, their basic purpose was repelling the Demon threat, so she permitted them, and that will-based direction was determined and accepted by the Labyrinth side. Indeed… both anti-Demon facilities and therapeutic baths are probably unrelated to Labyrinth maintenance.

“In that case, I look forward to working with you,” Claudia said, extending her hand to Tephra.

“The pleasure is mine. Goddess of the Moon. It’s an honor to meet you.”

Tephra smiled and took Claudia’s hand.

“I swear that as long as my contract with Claudia and my bond with my friend Theodore remain strong, I shall bring Blessings to this land.”

“Then I shall welcome that. Let us walk together and wish for each other’s prosperity.”

A radiance bloomed between Claudia and Tephra’s joined hands.

The light grew steadily brighter, becoming dazzlingly brilliant. Gradually, it slowly subsided.

“—That should do it. The area around this ritual site should have become something like an enclave of Mt. Tephra.”

“Meaning?”

“Tephra should be able to travel freely between the mountain and the ritual site now.”

“My, my.”

Tephra looked delighted at Claudia’s words.

“Hmm… So now the ritual site becomes Tephra’s Spirit Shrine, and we can develop the interior for convenient use as hot spring facilities.”

“That sounds enjoyable.”

I’ll have Alfred handle various aspects through Magic Construction for that. The area around the ritual site could probably become therapeutic baths or public bathhouses… Well, I’ll discuss it with King Melvin.

“Hot springs? How wonderful,” Grace said, and Marlene nodded vigorously. Everyone looked happy hearing about the hot springs. Yeah. I’m looking forward to the hot springs too. I’ll consult with Alfred and strive to create excellent facilities.

+++

# **231 – Blue Sky and Steam**

“Now then, Ambassador. I must head to the Royal Castle and request an audience with His Majesty Melvin.”

It seems Marquis Zilbolt is leaving the ritual grounds with his wife and daughter.

There are procedures to handle, like transferring custody of Elmer and the others.

“Understood. I may come to speak with you another day.”

“Very well. Let me thank you again for saving Elmer and the others.”

Marquis Zilbolt bowed once, then departed for the Royal Castle under the escort of his Knight Order.

Now then… When I looked toward the garden to see what happened after Claudia and Tephra made their contract, changes had already occurred. I could see hot water bubbling up from around the center of the pond.

Using Water Magic, I drew some water from near the spring to examine it. The temperature of the emerging water seemed relatively high. It might be just right for drawing to various places for use.

“No smell of hydrogen sulfide. Hmm.”

Though I think that smell also adds to the hot spring experience… Preferences vary from person to person.

I tasted it too. Tasteless and odorless—or so it seemed, but there was a faint sweetness. Hmm… It appears to contain a slight amount of Magical Power. It definitely seems to have medicinal properties.

“The changes are already happening.”

Everyone came to see for themselves.

“Indeed. We need to do something before the pond overflows.”

“That’s right. It’ll get flooded.”

“After we develop the surrounding area, we can simply draw the hot water there. But for now… diverting it to the river or sea would likely cause various impacts.”

Temperature changes and water quality changes. Since these elements weren’t there before, it might affect the ecosystem. I don’t usually concern myself with such details, but I wouldn’t want to affect the residents’ lives, and it probably isn’t what Tephra, as a Spirit, wants either.

“Hmm… Indeed, perhaps I was a bit hasty. The output depends on my power, but I believe I can adjust it to some extent.”

So the flow rate depends on Tephra. If the hot spring becomes famous and attracts people, Tephra’s power will likely increase.

“We can’t exactly monitor it constantly, so why not divert it to the Labyrinth side?”

Claudia suggested.

“Ah, using the sewer system?”

“That would be it. Since the hot spring water has different properties from what was there before, it might create a new section in the lower levels of the Labyrinth. But that in itself doesn’t affect the outside, so it shouldn’t be a problem.”

“I see. That’s interesting.”

I heard some slightly unsettling words like “new section”… but this place is already like a new section of the Labyrinth anyway. Since Claudia and Tephra seem fine with it, I decided to adopt that plan.

We extended an underground passage from the ritual grounds toward the Termwills side. We reinforced the surroundings to prevent leaks and connected it to the sewer system.

To prevent it from being used as an entrance/exit to the city interior, we modified the passage from the sewer outlet back toward the ritual grounds to a size impassable by people. Then we slightly altered the shape of the pond’s edge, creating a channel on the lower side and connecting it to the underground passage, completing the drainage route. It’s temporary, but it should suffice for the time being.

While we’re at it, let’s adjust the area around the spring too. We solidified and Petrified the pond bottom, remodeling it to prevent the water from getting muddy.

“Somehow, it seems like we could use it as a bath even as it is now.”

Irmhild said while lightly touching the water.

“I would like you all to be the first to enjoy it.”

Hmm… Well, if that’s the case, I’ll take them up on the offer of the first bath.

“Then let’s do that. The spring itself is hot, so we need to be a bit careful.”

When I said that, everyone’s faces lit up with joy.

“Then I’ll go get bath supplies from the house.”

“Understood. I’ll set up partitions and make other preparations.”

Taking a bath while the sun is still high has its own charm. Although the partitions block the view from the surroundings, so it doesn’t have the feel of an open-air bath, seeing the blue sky feels pleasant.

Just like at the lake before, everyone changed into swimsuits for bathing. The water temperature was somewhat hot, but not unbearably so.

I submerged myself up to the shoulders. I was enveloped in a comforting warmth that seemed to seep deep into my body.

“Ahh.”

I unintentionally let out a sound.

“How is the temperature?”

Tephra asked while also soaking in the water.

“Just right.”

“Good. That’s excellent to hear.”

When I answered, Tephra nodded with satisfaction. Seraphina was floating on her back on the water surface, looking very comfortable. The area around the ritual grounds was originally a comfortable place for Spirits and Fairies.

Since Lavigne dislikes hot water, we made a shallow bathtub, drew hot spring water into it, and cooled it to create a cold spring. The way she’s soaking heavily and not moving suggests she seems to like it in her own way.

“Mmm. Good water.”

“Really…”

Irmhild let out a big breath in response to Sheila’s murmur. She seems to have released her Humanization Spell and is relaxing leisurely.

“Theodore-sama. How are your injuries?”

Ashley inquired.

“Ah, yes. The burns don’t hurt anymore either.”

When I answered, everyone gathered around, apparently concerned about my wounds’ condition.

Somehow… even though everyone is wearing swimsuits, being surrounded by everyone with their faces flushed pink from the hot spring is… quite a stimulating sight.

Their wet skin glistens in the sunlight. Everyone has fair, fine-textured skin, so when their circulation improves, it becomes even more noticeable and alluring.

“At this rate, the Healing Shell might no longer be necessary.”

Trying it out, I peeled off the Healing Shell to find the burns already healing with new skin forming.

“At this rate, it seems there won’t even be scars. The cuts seem fine too.”

“Now that you mention it, I’ve heard some hot springs are effective for burns as well.”

Rosemary tilted her head.

“Indeed. Those who live near the mountains said it’s effective for burns too. It supposedly heals skin diseases and improves skin texture as well.”

Effective for burns too, huh? Then I’ll take my time soaking.

Triggered by Tephra’s words, the female members started getting excited, touching each other’s skin, commenting on how smooth it felt or how beautiful the fine texture was.

“Rosemary-sama, your skin is so beautiful.”

“Oh my, hearing that from you makes me happy, Grace. Though I envy the fairness of your and Ashley’s skin.”

“Claudia-sama’s skin is so smooth too.”

At Ashley’s words, Marlene began stroking Claudia’s arm, and so on. They seemed to be having quite a good time.

“Theodore seems to have rather nice skin too.”

At Sheila’s comment, everyone’s gaze turned toward me.

“Mmm. It’s true. It’s smooth.”

Seraphina, who had been floating nearby, stroked my shoulder as she said this.

“Ah, well… Mine is different from everyone else’s, or rather…”

Even as I answered, everyone laughed mischievously.

The flow seemed to Shift toward everyone touching my skin. My sides, my back—everywhere was being stroked by everyone’s hands.

…It was ticklish, and skin tones occupied most of my field of vision, making everything a blur. It’s good that everyone seems to be enjoying themselves, but… I should get out of the water before I get too flushed. Yeah.

Hmm. It was better water than I expected.

After getting out of the hot spring, I relaxed in one of the rooms of the facility we’d built for the Shrine Maidens’ stay. Some parts still lacked interior finishing and furniture, but it was sufficient for resting.

As for the hot spring, Penelope and the other Shrine Maidens were using it now. Their cheerful voices could be heard from the garden direction. Later, I’ll call the workshop and merchant guild members, Cecilia, Mihaela, and the Labyrinth Village residents too.

The area around the spring also has Tephra’s Spirit Shrine. Even if we draw water from here to various places, it might be best to keep the current facilities for use by our inner circle and royalty. First, let’s draw water into this facility and build a large bathhouse.

“My skin feels so moist.”

“It really does. Better than expected.”

Grace and Rosemary exchanged smiles.

“At this rate, we might be able to attract visitors for hot spring cures.”

“I’m sure of it. I think Father would be pleased too.”

Saying this, Rosemary laughed. Hmm. If we build various facilities around the hot spring, we’ll need staff to maintain them… Like the theater, this could become a good source of employment for the Orphanage members and Labyrinth Village residents.

Various ideas come to mind… but for now, should we separate the cure resort and the public bathhouse? Those seeking treatment would probably want a quiet stay, while public baths have an entertainment aspect.

+++

# **232 – Political Change in the Magical Kingdom**

Discussions with Marquis Zilbolt, evidence left behind by the witch, hot spring area development… There was a mountain of matters to discuss. I headed to the Royal Castle to speak with King Melvin.

Since Marquis Zilbolt would also be participating in this discussion, we were to meet in a room at the Guesthouse.

I knocked and entered. Marquis Zilbolt seemed to have arrived first.

“Ah, Ambassador.”

“Good day. How are your wife and daughter doing since then?”

I had gotten the impression that the lady and her daughter were somewhat delicate. If Alvelinde’s Curse Magic had caused them mental strain and made them less active, then I thought things should have been resolved now that everything was settled.

“Thanks to you, they’ve been showing smiles more often.”

“That’s wonderful to hear.”

Marquis Zilbolt placed a hand on his chest and smiled quietly. Then King Melvin arrived as well.

“Hmm. Have I kept you waiting?”

“I just arrived myself.”

We sat around the table, sipping from teacups as we talked.

“Well then. Where should we begin? First—Marquis Zilbolt. I’d like to hear what you know, if you don’t mind? That said, you’re not a noble serving me, but a vassal of the Silvatoria royal family. I only need information regarding Crown Prince Zadias’s schemes against our nation and anything related to demons.”

Marquis Zilbolt seemed to have an Intelligence Unit. Having been threatened by the Crown Prince, he had probably sent spies everywhere and gathered various pieces of information. But it wouldn’t do to have him share unrelated matters just because we helped him.

This touched upon the trust between King Melvin and Marquis Zilbolt, so it was probably best to draw a line there. However, when it came to matters involving demons, there was justification for cooperation across national borders.

“Understood. The Crown Prince came to my territory under the pretext of taking the waters. We welcomed him as a guest of honor… but the witch also appeared at that evening’s banquet. That was three years ago.”

And then the Curse Magic was cast on them. Judging from the preparations, he had probably used Curse Magic on Tephra first before coming to the Marquis’s place.

“From there, it’s as you can imagine. I did as I was told, gathering information about nobles within the country and carrying out various covert activities. However… I had no idea demons were involved behind the scenes…”

So he didn’t know about the connection between the Crown Prince and the demons. Well… From the Crown Prince’s perspective, even though he had leverage over the Marquis, he would want to avoid letting him know about his connections with demons.

“What about operations within the Kingdom of Verdugal? First, regarding the matter of the Thief group.”

“I was told to disguise them as thieves and establish bases. In the same way that minor clashes between nobles often involve organizing privateer Thief groups, I received those instructions.”

And so various preparations were made. Disguising themselves as merchants to transport supplies, sending Earth Magic-specialized Magicians into the mountains to create hideouts. Seizing one town, and then if they could control the volcano, they could cause Confusion within the Kingdom of Verdugal, inflict significant damage… Various sabotage operations were possible, and blackmail was certainly feasible.

“Considering the witch’s methods, we believe they intended to secure the dormant volcano and use it for similar threats against our nation. They probably planned to do so during this visit.”

“Is… that so. They even specified which strategic points to secure, so that must indeed be the case. I have no words to excuse myself.”

Marquis Zilbolt closed his eyes.

“I’m not blaming you. What about regarding Gartner County?”

“The Crown Prince told me to search for Magic that should be possessed by a Magician named Patricia. A Magician with tea-colored hair and golden eyes…”

He looked at me as he spoke. Given the appearance and the Gartner surname, Marquis Zilbolt had probably already guessed my connection to this. Well, there was no point in hiding it.

“Indeed… she might be the same person as my Mother.”

If we focus on the possibility that Patricia and Mother might be the same person… it shouldn’t be too difficult to track her down.

No, wait. But… ‘Saint Lisa’ has considerable fame within the Kingdom of Verdugal. It’s strange that he didn’t notice any connection to me at all.

“One question—regarding her whereabouts, did you gather information yourself and trace her to Gartner County?”

“No. It seems the Crown Prince was investigating Lady Patricia on his own as well. He said he had tracked her movements as far as Gartner County, and told me to search for her locally from there.”

“…When was this?”

“Recently. I received the information and immediately mobilized my unit.”

So that’s how it was, I should say. Based on the Crown Prince’s information, the Marquis and his people merely acted as the operational unit. Well, if that’s the case, then the scarcity of information they possess makes sense, doesn’t it?

That leaves the question of where the Crown Prince obtained his information from—

“Regarding this Lady Patricia… based on combining various rumors and speculation, we believe she might have been driven out of the country during Silvatoria’s political upheaval.”

“Political upheaval…”

“While this concerns Silvatoria’s internal affairs, if you have any knowledge, could you share it?”

Marquis Zilbolt seemed hesitant, but after shaking his head slightly, he spoke.

“That is probably… referring to the Faction Conflict at the Academy.”

“The Sages’ Academy?”

“Yes. I too received instruction at the Academy in my youth. It’s similar to the renowned Peresford Academy in the Kingdom of Verdugal… but its distinguishing feature is its specialization in Magic.”

The mainstream Tower Magician Guild advocates “Magic for daily life” and seeks to widely disseminate Magic. However, the Sages’ Academy in Silvatoria maintains secrecy, rarely making Magical Technology available to the public. Instead, it boasts of elite training and has produced many famous Magicians.

“The Crown Prince was also enrolled there. However… the Crown Prince joined forces with the Vice Chancellor at that time and criticized the Academy’s Chancellor and elders. He argued that to develop the nation, all secretly held technologies should be disclosed.”

…I see. So the Crown Prince pressured the Academy under the pretext of national development.

“And what happened?”

“The Chancellor and elders resisted this. Conflict broke out between the Chancellor faction and Vice Chancellor faction. Shortly after, the Chancellor’s accidental death and the Crown Prince’s attempted assassination occurred in quick succession… Each side blamed the other. Tensions rose, but eventually the Magic Knight Order intervened with military force on the Academy’s side. Many Magicians from the Chancellor faction were killed or injured, and several elders were imprisoned.”

In other words… the Crown Prince’s side won through military backing.

“What about within the court nobility?”

“Among the court nobles who were close with the Chancellor, some were suspected of involvement in the Crown Prince’s attempted assassination and were imprisoned or executed. However… due to the Academy’s secretive nature and the Crown Prince’s military intervention into the magic research institution, the matter was pushed toward concealment. As a result—it was reframed as a power struggle among court nobles, that is, under the pretext of a political upheaval.”

“I see…”

They probably wanted to avoid increasing negative publicity about Silvatoria or the Crown Prince.

Originally, matters concerning the Academy belonged to the highest secrets of the magic superpower. The information concealment was somewhat successful, with only information about power struggles leaking out.

“If Lady Patricia, who fled Silvatoria, possesses valuable Magic… she’s probably either a relative of the deceased Chancellor or his faction, or an elder’s close relative or distinguished disciple.”

“What about Teleportation Magic? How is it known?”

Claudia had already shown it to Marquis Zilbolt. At this point, there was no use hiding that aspect.

“It was said the tradition died out long ago. Due to the Academy’s secrecy, there were rumors that the elders might be hiding the Spell Formula as secret teachings. …Regarding the Teleportation Magic I witnessed the other day, I swear to take it to my grave.”

“I appreciate your understanding.”

I don’t know how he’s taking the matter about Claudia, but explaining that might just complicate things further.

“The issue is how to deal with the Crown Prince. We must also ensure Marquis Zilbolt’s safety…”

That’s right. That’s the problem from now on. Investigating the connection between the Crown Prince and demons is fine. But it would be meaningless if the Marquis ends up being made a scapegoat.

“Regarding that matter—Spirit Tephra said she would protect the Marquis and testify to his innocence.”

“That’s reassuring. Of course, I too shall endeavor to prove the Marquis’s innocence.”

Yes. With the testimony of the King of Verdugal and a High Spirit. And if the perpetrator turns out to be a demon. Once that becomes widely known, it would become very difficult to target the Marquis himself. The Crown Prince’s bad reputation is partly due to his tough measures against the Academy, so at the very least, keeping things in the shadows would be impossible. Still, we need a strategy to make it difficult for the Crown Prince himself to act.

“What if we deliberately don’t mention the Crown Prince’s name or connections, and instead announce that this witch was the perpetrator of the attempted assassination of the Marquis’s family?”

“Oh?”

“Along with her description, we announce that this witch was actually a demon. And that among the demon’s possessions was a pass issued by Silvatoria.”

“So we let them investigate the facts themselves. Hmm… If it becomes a major issue, they won’t be able to use the excuse that the King is ill in bed. The Crown Prince will be busy putting out fires, and with suspicion cast within Silvatoria, it would be difficult for them to find pretexts to stop our intention to deliver it directly.”

King Melvin grinned. Then for a while, he seemed to be thinking with his arms crossed, but eventually nodded.

“Very well. When the Marquis returns to his country, we shall provide him with an Escort. I will make the arrangements, so you should remain in our nation for a while. Should anything happen, I won’t let harm come to you.”

“I am deeply grateful for your consideration.”

Marquis Zilbolt bowed his head deeply.

From the Crown Prince’s perspective, he’s waiting for the witch’s return. Even if they have means of communication, as long as the Crown Prince can’t openly acknowledge the witch, he can’t act overtly. As long as Marquis Zilbolt is scheduled to stay in the Kingdom of Verdugal, we have plenty of time to prepare.

+++

# **233 – The Dwelling of the Water Dragon**

King Melvin said he would proceed with measures around Silvatoria.

That aside… I still had one urgent task remaining.

“I think I’ll first make sure to properly finish the Magic Light Water Vein matter.”

“Hmm… I hope no demons interfere this time. I’ll deploy personnel as planned, but… there was some issue with the Magic Light Water Vein, wasn’t there?”

“According to her story, yes.”

The unsealing of the sealed door in the Magic Light Water Vein was only days away. There was no doubt Alvelinde had connections with those demons.

I anticipated combat would occur before the unsealing. While the possibility of interference during the actual event was probably low, that didn’t mean we could let our guard down. According to Claudia, the Water Spirit Hall was different from the others, with a somewhat unusual Guardian.

“Still, I don’t think there will be many problems. My injuries are mostly healed… I’ll focus on making sure my physical condition is perfect for the day.”

At my words, King Melvin’s expression darkened for a moment. Hmm. He seemed troubled by the situation where I was the only one who could handle high-ranking demons.

Well then, perhaps I should change the subject.

“Ah, about the ritual site matter…”

As I changed both my tone and the topic, King Melvin smiled somewhat awkwardly. I had already contacted him about the ritual site matter via communication device. While we weren’t being careless, this was a situation where we could use some brighter topics.

“…You mentioned a hot spring had sprung up, correct?”

“Yes. I’m thinking of developing the surrounding area. I’d like to build a therapeutic bathhouse and public bathhouse, among other things.”

This was business as usual. I wanted to quickly create a model, have the necessary materials prepared, and begin construction.

“Who manages the current public bathhouses?”

“That falls under the jurisdiction of the officials.”

Hmm… In that case, maybe I don’t need to worry about competitors?

According to King Melvin, while bathhouses have aspects of public entertainment, they’re facilities intended to promote awareness of maintaining cleanliness and the accompanying aesthetic upkeep. In short, they’re for welfare benefits and also serve the public good.

Hence, they’re managed by the state. The bathing facilities found here and there are the same.

“However, they’re not operated by that many hands. If we expand the scale, we’ll need to increase personnel. Let’s see… We can decide gradually while looking at the facility’s scale.”

This aspect is similar to the theater. Regarding the development around the ritual site, fiddling with the scale model serves as magic control training, so I’ll work on it during my free time.

“The Spirit Hall… I wonder what’s beyond the door?”

As we gathered in the workshop to discuss plans for the Magic Light Water Vein unsealing day, Rosemary voiced her question. This would be Rosemary’s first time going to a Spirit Hall. I needed to explain in detail.

“Based on previous locations—it feels like there’s a temple-like building in the opened area.”

“The terrain beyond the door differs according to the section, but the building forms are consistent with previous ones. The Verdgar royal family side at that time also deployed the Spirit Hall Guardians in the same way. However… the Water Spirit Hall has some differences from previous ones.”

Claudia supplemented my words.

“Is there some problem?”

Alfred tilted his head while inspecting his equipment.

“The Verdgar king at that time protected a mated pair of water dragons that had been injured in the nearby sea and washed ashore on the beach. Several spell formulas for using the labyrinth remained from that era. During the sanctuary ritual, permission was requested to incorporate external monsters. This included not just golems, but those water dragons as well.”

Water dragons. And a mated pair at that.

Unlike the classification of sub-dragons like wyverns and earth dragons used for riding, these are genuine dragon species. However, they’re said to have gentle temperaments. Since they mainly eat fish and shellfish, they rarely become hostile toward humans… but they possess power worthy of being called dragons.

Indeed… considering their longevity and strength, they would be perfect as guardians for the Orb.

“Due to attacks by demons, the water dragons were wounded and lost their child. So they’re cooperative about sealing the demons. They alternate between dormancy and activity… during active periods, they feed on other labyrinth monsters in the deep floors of the Magic Light Water Vein.”

I had thought the Magic Light Water Vein was strangely rich in ingredients… but hearing this, it might also function as a feeding ground for the water dragons.

“So the demons attacked even the water dragons…”

“I heard there was someone who tried to capture their child to subjugate it.”

The result was combat with the water dragons trying to reclaim their child, during which the water dragons were wounded and the child got caught in the fighting and died.

“Well, if we belong to the royal family or labyrinth side, we probably won’t have to fight.”

“I see…”

“Even so, we can’t let our guard down just because we’ve defeated demons before.”

At Grace’s words, everyone nodded with serious expressions.

We’ve been properly progressing with training. As the date approaches, rather than focusing on training, it becomes more important to maintain physical condition and thoroughly prepare, checking that equipment isn’t deteriorating. Especially since our group has many magic tools.

“After the Magic Light Water Vein matter is finished, we’ll proceed with things around the ritual site too. Knowing Theo-kun, you’re probably thinking about various things, right?”

Alfred seemed to have finished inspecting the magic tools’ circuits and operation, and asked me that.

“Well, to some extent.”

I’ve reached the stage where I can write down spell formulas to have them made into magic tools. I need to work on that during spare moments too.

—And then the day arrived when the Magic Light Water Vein’s seal would be broken.

The Knight Order, Mage Corps, soldiers, and Adventurer Guild were on alert, creating a tense atmosphere.

Important facilities like the Royal Castle, areas around the Temple, and the ritual site were secured, with communication device holders dispersed throughout. They were preparing for unexpected situations while maintaining close contact.

Seeing off people like Mildred, Penelope, and Auria, I flew to the Magic Light Water Vein—passing through the underwater cave and heading toward the large hall where I fought Alvelinde.

The sound of flowing water and the sealed door. This place remained just as it was when I came before. The wall I destroyed with my magic had been neatly repaired. This aspect is unique to labyrinths.

As we waited, the appointed time arrived.

Light appeared on the sealed door’s relief, and its celestial chart began to move. As if cracking from the center, the door slowly opened—and water came rushing from the passage beyond.

We all gained altitude to ride out the rising water level. I could see many small fish mixed in the water. Schools of fish shining in various colors—. The rich colors reminded me of tropical seas.

As the schools of fish passed through with the water abundantly filled with magical power—shining crystals, corals, and such popped out everywhere, growing with tremendous speed. The previously empty large hall had instantly become quite lively.

Water was still continuously flowing from beyond the sealed door. For sea creatures, this must be blessed water.

The fish schools, along with the water that had rushed from the Spirit Hall, pushed forward through the Magic Light Water Vein’s underwater cave connecting to the large hall.

“That water will pass through the cave and reach the nearby sea. For a while, there might be abundant fishing not just in the Magic Light Water Vein, but around Termwills too.”

“…Now that you mention it, I heard the Magic Light Water Vein connects to the sea?”

“There aren’t exactly entrances, but it’s in the form of water gushing out from various places on the seabed.”

…I see. Anyway, the sealed door had opened. The communication devices reported no abnormalities. There was no sign of demons transferring in at the moment.

Exchanging glances and nodding with everyone, we advanced beyond the sealed door.

Proceeding deeper and deeper along the half-submerged passage, our view opened up.

“Beautiful…”

Ashley inadvertently let out an admiring voice. Everyone else seemed speechless too. A space even more vast than previous Spirit Halls. Fitting for being the water dragons’ roost.

But most of it seemed submerged. The Spirit Hall was also half-submerged, with stepping stone-like footholds continuing sporadically.

Shining crystals protruded from the walls and ceiling, illuminating the water bottom that resembled an underground lake. …No wonder fish schools emerged. Vividly colored seaweed, purple, orange, and pink corals, countless small fish—. My, my. What an incredible sight.

From its depths, large white shadows swayed. Two shadows. The water dragons.

…Somehow, seaweed and corals were growing on their backs. They’d become habitats for the fish.

The two water dragons with pure white bodies and blue eyes slowly surfaced, then extended their long necks from the water and looked at us.

They didn’t seem to have any intention of attacking—. Well then.

+++

# **234 – Dragon Scales**

“It’s been a long time, Claudia.”

“I didn’t expect you to visit me immediately after the seal was released.”

I heard calm male and female voices. The voices didn’t seem to come from the water dragons’ mouths but rather from somewhere else. I could faintly hear extremely high-pitched sounds at the edge of human hearing. They were probably using some kind of magic to communicate.

“Yes. Good morning. How are you feeling after waking up?”

At Claudia’s question, the water dragons narrowed their eyes. They seemed to be acquainted with Claudia.

“Not bad.”

“Though I am somewhat hungry.”

Claudia laughed at the male dragon’s slightly joking tone.

“That’s wonderful to hear. May I introduce you to each other?”

After the water dragons nodded, Claudia introduced us to each other. The water dragons were a married couple – the husband was Pernas and the wife was Invel.

I was introduced as her fiancé… but the dragon couple stared at me with great interest.

“I see… Is that why you’re traveling with the princesses of the royal family?”

Claudia gave a wry smile at Invel’s words.

“That’s part of it. May we receive the Orb?”

“If both the master of the labyrinth and members of the Verdgar royal family have come to receive the Orb, we have no objections.”

“After all, we agreed to cooperate for this very purpose.”

“Thank you.”

Throughout Verdgar’s long history, there seem to have been various kings. Some were wise kings like King Melvin, while others were tyrants.

As a result, there were generations where the traditions were lost. However, Claudia, who desired stability and the safety of the Labyrinth Village, never actively involved herself with the royal family despite her internal conflicts.

So… while the royal family might have forgotten about these water dragons… the water dragons probably haven’t forgotten their promise with the royal family.

I wanted to ask more about the Orb, but as I was thinking that, they turned their gaze toward me.

“We don’t mind handing over the Orb… but we’d like to speak with your fiancé for a moment. Would that be alright?”

“I don’t mind. I wanted to ask you some questions too. In the meantime, could you retrieve the Orb? It doesn’t seem like there are any Golems or Gargoyles stationed here.”

“Understood.”

At my words, everyone headed toward the Spirit Hall. After watching their backs, I turned to face the water dragons.

“You don’t seem intimidated facing us alone. That’s commendable courage.”

“Well… if I got scared fighting demons, I wouldn’t get anywhere.”

“Is that so. You fight demons… The refinement of your magical power, to reach that level…”

Invel narrowed her eyes as if trying to see something through the light, looking slightly dazzled.

“We’re quite surprised by this. You could say we’re interested in you. That Claudia would travel with the princesses and smile so gently…”

“Claudia was always kind. I think she recognized that she tended to be too lenient with herself, which might be why she tried not to get too involved.”

Even though she was badly betrayed and tried not to get involved, I think she came out because she was worried as the seal release approached. The fact remains unchanged that she has consistently been an ally of the surface people and has continued to protect the residents of the Labyrinth Village.

“…Perhaps you’re right. We too are not eternal. Our living places are different. Once we fall asleep, we won’t be able to meet for a while.”

“That’s why we wanted to speak with you.”

I see… They’re worried about Claudia.

“I want to destroy the Last Guardian and free Claudia from the labyrinth.”

“I see…”

Invel closed her eyes as she spoke.

“May I ask you about the Orb and the Miasma Orb too?”

When I asked, both of them nodded.

“However, we cannot guarantee we know what you wish to learn.”

“Our promise with the royal family was to protect the four Orbs.”

“Not just the one here?”

“Indeed. When the Orbs fall into the hands of wrongdoers, we are to reveal their location to the royal family and retrieve them if necessary. Therefore, we are not particularly knowledgeable about the seals. Probably to prevent too much information from being extracted from us.”

Probably because if they went outside, they didn’t know what would happen if they fought demons. In fact, they seem to have been wounded in battles with demons before. So by cooperating with the royal family – I think there’s also the purpose of preserving the traditions about the Orbs.

In exchange for being bound by this duty, the water dragons have made this Magic Light Water Vein their peaceful home.

As Guardians of the Water Spirit Hall, they can teleport anywhere within the Magic Light Water Vein. They can even emerge near the Termwills coast… This aspect is similar to Tephra. Even though they’re bound by contract to protect the Orb, they don’t seem particularly restricted.

Still… the water dragons know the locations of the Orbs.

Then I should assume they can do the same with the Miasma Orbs. There are indeed risks in hiding or destroying the Miasma Orbs.

“What about the demons from that time?”

“Those beings haven’t changed since ancient times… but during the era when there was a leader, they seemed more organized than now.”

“What kind of power does the leader have? I don’t think they’d follow someone just because they’re strong.”

“The leader was said to guide demons toward awakening. However, there’s no comparison between lower demons awakened by the leader and high-ranking demons who achieved awakening on their own.”

I see. The flowering of each demon’s abilities.

Being able to raise the overall combat power is indeed threatening. It leads to strengthening the demon species as a whole, not just individuals. Also, the water dragons might not know everything about the leader.

“I’m sorry our information isn’t more helpful.”

“No, it was useful.”

“Please wait a moment.”

Invel dove into the water… and returned after a while. She placed what she was holding in her mouth on the platform.

This is – scales? And multiple ones at that.

“We hear humans value our scales and fangs. These are from our last molting, and we tried to select the best condition ones… but can these be of any use to you?”

“More than enough.”

Dragon scales. If processed, they can be used for both weapons and armor. I need to consider various uses.

Grace and the others returned from the Spirit Hall. The Orb was shining in their hands.

“We will always be here. If there’s anything we can help with, please come anytime. If you set foot in this place, we will know.”

After exchanging these words, the water dragons slowly swam toward the vast space extending behind the Spirit Hall. Along the way, another one – a small water dragon – appeared.

Turning around, the family bowed as if in greeting before disappearing into the water. …I see. So they’re a family of three now.

My eyes met with everyone who was watching the water dragons depart with narrowed eyes. Everyone seemed to have their own thoughts about the scene – about the water dragons’ circumstances, their faithfulness in still keeping promises made so long ago.

“Shall we return?”

“–Yes.”

When I said this, everyone smiled and nodded.

“Dragon scales…!”

“And water dragon scales at that–!”

We delivered the Orb to the Royal Castle and reported on the outcome of this mission. Afterward, I brought the dragon scales to the workshop.

Viola and Miriam’s excitement upon seeing the dragon scales was quite impressive. Miriam had come to report since she had finished various arrangements for toy orders placed through the merchant guild.

“May we touch them?”

“Go ahead.”

When I answered, the two picked up the scales and cheered.

“Ooooh…!”

“They’re light–! So light! I thought they’d be heavier!”

They remained excited the whole time.

“How should we process them?”

Alfred showed a wry smile at the scene.

“Hmm… First, armor, I think. Like chest protectors that can be worn under clothing.”

After all, we have enough for all Party Members. Given their thickness and lightness, they shouldn’t hinder movement. We want armor that can particularly protect vital areas like the neck, heart, and spine. And if we apply Enchantment, it should significantly improve defensive capabilities.

After equipping everyone with armor, we can use the leftover pieces for Irmhild’s giant arrowheads or to reinforce the edges of Marlene’s Saucer. This should allow for a good enhancement of our combat strength.

“Understood. Then we’ll focus on equipping armor first.”

“Right. And about the Magic Tools around the ritual site… well, I’ve been thinking of several ideas. Spell Formulas for creating bubbles, for drawing up or flowing water. I’ll demonstrate them for you later.”

“I’m looking forward to that.”

“Though they’re not particularly high Difficulty Techniques.”

For the main attraction of the public bath, we want to prepare jacuzzis, water slides, saunas, and such. By offering rare entertainment at the public bath and charging admission fees, while keeping the therapeutic baths free of such things and maintaining them as places for medical treatment, we can clearly differentiate between the two.

+++

# **235 – New District of Termwills**

“Alright. Shall we begin then?”

Leaving through the Eastern District gate early in the morning, I headed to the construction site. Rotating my arms lightly and cracking my neck, it was time to start work.

First, the outer wall. Next, the underground sewer system, then the main street. The hot spring facilities would come after ensuring safety at the construction site and completing the infrastructure. Once those aspects were taken care of, the construction of the new district should progress rapidly.

The work began from one section of the outer wall. First, I would turn the parts corresponding to the outer moat into Golems, then use those Golems as material for the outer wall. Using Petrification Magic to turn them into stone, I repeated the process of stacking, hardening, and reinforcing, matching the height as I extended the outer wall.

I could keenly feel the gazes from Merchants and others lining up in front of the gate trying to enter Termwills… but I shouldn’t pay too much attention to it.

Well, what can I say. While the outer wall is a massive structure compared to something like the theater, its structure is ultimately simple. It’s just a matter of creating guard posts for soldiers and watchtowers at regular intervals, plus making pathways for movement along the top.

The structure in this area is… well, just improving the precision based on the existing outer wall. What requires the most care is the exterior. Removing any handholds to prevent climbing. Filling the gaps between stones so tightly that not even a sheet of paper could slip through.

Caduceus, transformed into a bird, was flying around overhead. This was to verify from a bird’s-eye view whether the outer wall was being constructed according to the scaled model.

“This should make climbing difficult.”

Sheila said while touching the surface of the sheer vertical wall. Attacks by foreign tribes or bandits are virtually nonexistent within Verdgar’s central territory. If asked what the outer wall is preparing against, it would primarily be a defense against Monsters.

“What about you, Irm? How is it?”

I asked Irmhild, who was on the upper pathway of the outer wall. Irmhild had been testing the pathway’s usability – drawing a Bow from behind cover, making motions as if shooting an arrow, then hiding again – but eventually nodded.

“Hmm. I think it’s good. I thought the cover walls might be a bit high, but probably most soldiers are taller than me, so this height should be fine.”

I see. Then let’s proceed like this.

The hot spring town that will become the new district isn’t particularly large in scale. So the extension distance for the outer wall isn’t that significant either… well, probably finished before noon. Once this is done, next is the underground sewer system. This time, by using the excavated material from that sewer to pave stone roads, the main street will be essentially complete.

“This is… astonishing. I never imagined you’d already extended the outer wall this much. And this smoothness of the wall…”

While I was progressing with the work, around noon, it was Chancellor Howard who arrived. According to what King Melvin told me, Howard loves hot springs and is apparently incredibly excited about the new district.

“Well, the material is just the earth and sand from the outer moat. Since digging the moat and procuring materials for the outer wall happen simultaneously, it’s progressing reasonably well.”

“Is that so, is that so.”

Howard had a beaming expression. I heard he usually refrains from direct contact with me as one of King Melvin’s direct vassals… but his love for hot springs seems genuine.

According to King Melvin – after the theater’s Great Success, there was talk that if I built a public bathhouse, good attendance could be expected, so starting with the hot spring-loving chancellor, the senior officials are quite enthusiastic. Apparently, that discussion even developed to the point of adding one more district to Termwills, albeit small-scale.

In essence, since people will likely gather, Verdgar is putting serious effort into properly developing the area. That’s why even while I’m building like this, materials are being rapidly transported in at an accelerated pace.

Currently, an area around the ritual site is generating a Barrier similar to that of a Temple, thanks to the power of Spirits and the Moon Goddess. Once the outer wall extension is complete, the hot spring town should become quite secure in terms of security. The ritual site is a facility where Shrine Maidens are stationed at the Tephra Shrine. It was originally planned to be walled off from a crime prevention perspective anyway.

The main street running through the center of the hot spring town. Public bathhouses in the central area of the hot spring town. A plaza with a fountain. Accommodation facilities and a Market arranged. The Tephra Shrine located slightly away from the center. Further out, therapeutic bath facilities. A stay facility doubling as a clinic, allowing those coming for the therapeutic baths to rest quietly and recuperate.

Following these construction plans, after enclosing with the outer wall, the next step is to lay sewer pipes throughout the new district. Digging, hardening, and finally making it flow into Termwills’ sewer system.

“My, the famously rumored Otherworld Ambassador’s Magic Construction… I’ve truly enjoyed witnessing it.”

The chancellor watched my outer wall construction for a while, but eventually seemed satisfied, nodding with a cheerful demeanor.

“I’m afraid I cannot attend to you properly.”

“No, no. If I were to barge in uninvited and furthermore disturb the Otherworld Ambassador, I would receive His Majesty’s scolding. I’ll be cheering for the completion of the hot spring town from the shadows.”

Saying that, the chancellor left with his escort soldiers. The outer wall was completed not long after that. Now, all that remained was to create a passage in the original outer wall separating the hot spring town and Termwills’ town.

“Theo, lunch is ready.”

“Understood. I’ll be right there.”

Grace, who had been preparing lunch at the ritual site, came to call me.

Hmm… Finished before noon, as expected. At this rate, I should be able to start working on the sewer system and main street too.

After having lunch at the ritual site, we decided to gather at the gazebo for a short break and have tea together. Alfred and the others from the workshop also showed up at the ritual site.

“Theodore. I have something to discuss.”

While relaxing with a teacup, Claudia spoke.

“Hmm, what is it?”

“I want to visit Mt. Tephra once. Just as this place became an enclave of Mt. Tephra, if I make a contract with Tephra over there, by making a part of the mountain a pseudo-section of the Labyrinth, I can connect it here and enable transportation via teleportation.”

…Hmm. In that case, we could protect the people of the Zilbolt Marquis household and the Marquisate’s residents in an emergency. Unless we create stone monuments, only Claudia should be capable of teleportation between two points.

“But that would depend on whether Marquis Zilbolt agrees, right?”

Having a direct route from a foreign country within one’s territory… in the current situation, it would be reassuring as insurance, but for a lord, it means taking on risk.

“That would require making a contract with Marquis Zilbolt as well. How about entrusting the decision to seal and open the direct route to the Marquis?”

I see. Once the current situation calms down and the need is over, it can basically be sealed. They would hold the key, and only Claudia would have the means for transportation. Create an emergency passage, but once its purpose is served, neither side can use it. As for communication methods, we have Tephra even if we can’t provide Communication Devices.

“Would it not hinder my movement?”

“Tephra is just moving between her own mountain and the enclave. We’re creating a new path in the portion borrowed from Tephra, so it won’t interfere.”

“Then I have no objection.”

Tephra nodded as if relieved, then smiled and nibbled on the cookies Grace had baked. Somehow… Tephra seems to have taken a liking to the ritual site and is fitting in strangely well. The sight of Seraphina and Rosemary’s Familiar Ambrum relaxing together in the gazebo is quite an unusual combination.

“Speaking of the Marquisate of Zilbolt, it’s near the Marquisate of Fobrester, isn’t it? Across the sea, so to speak.”

Ashley said while tilting her head in recollection.

Come to think of it, there was that verbal promise too… about going to Marquis Fobrester’s place to train his Knight Order.

“…Should we accompany Marquis Zilbolt when he returns? Making it a form where we also visit Marquis Fobrester.”

If it’s for escorting Claudia and Tephra, well, that should be within the scope of my duties as Otherworld Ambassador.

“Then I’ll inform Ophelia. Since the envoy hasn’t been decided yet, there should be time to send a letter to Marquis Fobrester at least.”

Alfred said.

“An envoy, huh. The selection does seem difficult.”

There might be Demons involved, and half the purpose is going to complain to their Crown Prince, after all. The selection would have to be careful.

“Her Highness Stephania says she wants to go as the envoy herself… but it seems her father is trying to persuade her not to.”

“Stephania disliked Crown Prince Zadias. And since it seems there are people in Silvatoria she owes favors to, just watching with her hands tied must be frustrating for her.”

Rosemary analyzed Princess Stephania’s feelings like that.

The First Princess, Princess Stephania. She holds territory in the north and should be familiar with Silvatoria too. Indeed… given that it will be difficult negotiations, Princess Stephania might be the right person for the job. Still, King Melvin will likely show reluctance.

I don’t know how the persuasion will turn out, but if that happens, the selection of escorts will become important too.

Hmm… Once the maintenance is finished, should I make an appearance at the Royal Castle? Tephra will also accompany us to testify to Marquis Zilbolt’s innocence, and it’s already becoming an incident involving those Demons.

+++

# **236 – Helfrid's Proposal**

First, let’s finish the sewer and main street improvements.

As usual, I’ll use the excavated soil as materials for Golems while improving the sewers, then transform the Golems into cobblestones. The excess materials will be stacked in the storage area as construction materials. After roughly completing these improvements, I’ll create a therapeutic spa facility slightly away from the main street.

All the necessary materials are ready. Since the therapeutic spa is a facility for recuperation, it doesn’t need the kind of novel Magic Tools found in public baths. All that’s needed are bathtubs, foot baths, and facilities for rest and medical treatment, then piping in the hot spring water.

A wooden facility where many people can relax comfortably. I’ll make windows for good sunlight, create an inner garden visible from those windows, then surround the area with a wall to complete it. The interior decoration and furniture will be prepared separately.

“How’s this?”

“Mm-hmm. I think it’s fine.”

With Seraphina on my shoulder, we check the building’s structural integrity together. The outer walls, sewers, therapeutic spa – nothing seems particularly problematic.

Let’s return to the ritual site and inform everyone that I’ll be heading to the Royal Castle.

“The therapeutic spa is finished, so I’ll be going to the Royal Castle for a bit.”

“That’s impressively fast. I need to work harder too,” Alfred murmurs.

When we discussed the escort to Silvatoria, he seemed determined to complete everything before Marquis Zilbolt and I depart. A full set of Dragon Scale Armor plus hot spring-related Magic Tools – it seems quite challenging.

“Steph and I are helping too. We’ll definitely have it ready in time,” Talcott says.

“Well… just don’t overwork yourselves.”

“That’s right. When we get tired, we’ll continue working while enjoying the hot springs,” Alfred says with a laugh.

Heading to the Royal Castle, I wait as usual in the King’s Tower salon until King Melvin appears.

“I’ve come to report that the improvements around the hot spring town’s outer walls, sewers, and main streets, plus the construction of the therapeutic spa, are complete.”

“As always, your work is remarkably swift.”

King Melvin’s eyes widen slightly as he nods.

“But understood. Regarding the therapeutic spa, I’ll have the interior, furniture, and equipment prepared as scheduled. I’ll also arrange for pharmacists who can work at the facility.”

“Yes.”

While the therapeutic spa’s interior is one thing, the shops and houses to be built in the hot spring town from now on will be entrusted to Termwills residents from the construction stage. If the new district leads to job creation, well, I have no complaints either.

“If we put the hot spring town properties up for sale, applications would likely flood in. Howard was practically dancing with excitement about the hot springs and special demand.”

“Ah, the Prime Minister did come to check on the progress.”

“Indeed. That man is an unparalleled bath enthusiast. With hot springs involved, he’d be even more excited.”

King Melvin gives a wry smile. I see. Even though he’d been keeping his distance out of consideration for my position until now, he couldn’t resist the temptation of the hot springs. If he sees the finished jacuzzi, he might request one for his residence.

Well, that aside.

“Besides the hot spring progress, there’s something else I’d like to discuss. I spoke with Claudia—”

I explain to King Melvin what Claudia and I discussed.

“So for that reason, I’d like to visit Mt. Tephra once. Of course, only after speaking with Marquis Zilbolt and obtaining permission.”

“You’re also heading to Silvatoria?”

“That’s right. I think it will be in the form of escorting Claudia and Tephra.”

“Hmm…”

King Melvin places his hand on his chin, ponders for a moment, then nods.

“Very well. I’ll inquire about Marquis Zilbolt’s intentions myself.”

“Speaking of escorts, I heard about the messenger to Silvatoria.”

“Stephania? Certainly, she would be an ideal messenger in many respects, but there are aspects that make it difficult to agree. Given the nature of the matter.”

Since it involves Demons, there are risks in sending Princess Stephania.

“And you’re asking me about this here… does that mean you’re volunteering to escort Stephania?”

“I’ll be crossing over to Silvatoria and escorting Tephra as well. I can’t exactly separate from Claudia either. So I thought, in case of emergencies, we could keep Teleportation Magic as insurance.”

Emergencies. For example, if the Crown Prince has completely secured Silvatoria’s military power and launches a counterattack when cornered, or if Demons have infiltrated even the Royal Castle.

“Also… if we can secure their cooperation, I thought we might obtain information about Miasma Orbs.”

“I see…”

King Melvin closes his eyes, appearing to think much longer than before.

“I’ve become quite dependent on you, haven’t I?”

“It aligns with what I want to do myself.”

At my words, King Melvin shows a smile that could be either wry or self-deprecating before raising his head.

“There’s one promise I’d like you to make.”

“What would that be?”

“Even if you discover something, please don’t head to Beriondora alone. It would be too dangerous without understanding the situation.”

“Understood. I promise.”

Well… I am an escort. Not just regarding Beriondora, I’ll try to avoid reckless actions.

“Master. Sir Chester has arrived.”

After finishing my report to the Royal Castle and everyone had returned home to relax in the recreation room, Cecilia came to call me.

“Mm. Understood. I’ll head there immediately.”

It’s relatively rare for Chester to come to the house alone. I wonder what it’s about?

Heading to the reception room, I find Chester waiting, dressed not in his usual knight attire but in noble-style clothing.

“Good evening.”

“Pardon the late visit.”

Chester bows. As we sit facing each other, Claire the Arachne gracefully pours tea into teacups.

“Thank you.”

When I express my thanks, Claire smiles and withdraws to the corner of the room. Not just Claire, but recently everyone seems to be becoming more accustomed to their servant roles. This is probably thanks to Cecilia and Mihaela’s guidance.

Now, let’s hear what Chester has to say.

“What brings you here? It doesn’t seem like just a social visit.”

“That’s right. I’ve received a consultation from His Highness Helfried. I came to inquire about Sir Theodore’s intentions.”

A consultation from Prince Helfried.

“His Highness Helfried would like to speak with Sir Theodore about Rosemary-sama. Accordingly, he asked me to act as an intermediary. I apologize for the sudden request, but given His Highness Helfried’s short stay, I’d appreciate your understanding.”

“A conversation with me?”

Third Prince Helfried. He met my sister Rosemary once at the North Tower and was rather bluntly rejected. He probably hasn’t met with her since then…

“Um, His Highness Helfried was concerned that he might be disliked because he said something rude to Sir Theodore once before.”

“No. I received his apology.”

It wasn’t that big of a deal anyway. But if that’s the case, he probably doesn’t have any complaints against me either. Then it might be that he’s worried about my sister.

Certainly, having Chester, who visited the North Tower with him, act as an intermediary would be appropriate.

“His Highness said that if a meeting is possible, he will accommodate Sir Theodore’s schedule completely.”

“Understood. Should she be present as well?”

“He didn’t specify either way about that… but he did say it would be fine if Rosemary-sama learned about it. The matter concerns Rosemary-sama, I believe. He seemed quite worried.”

Hmm. Well, that makes sense. If Prince Helfried has something to discuss with me, it would be about Rosemary.

And Helfried’s stay in Termwills is short too… Hmm.

“Understood. …Well then. If sooner is better, then tomorrow afternoon at the ritual site. After that, it would have to be in the evening at the Royal Castle or my home.”

I promised Alfred I’d test the Magic Tools tomorrow. Alfred is somewhat busy too, so that’s not something I can cancel.

Besides, if he’s to understand Rosemary’s current situation, even though she needs the disguise Ring, it would be best for him to see that she can go out relatively freely.

“Understood. I’ll convey that to His Highness Helfried.”

“You can contact me through the Communication Device for your response.”

“Yes. Then I’ll ensure to contact you before it gets too late.”

Saying this, Chester bows deeply once more.

Well… I should probably tell Rosemary. Given Rosemary’s personality, if she hears about this, she’ll likely offer to be present, and it wouldn’t be right for her to be kept in the dark about her own matters.

+++

# **237 – The Prince's Concern**

The next day. I was scheduled to meet with Prince Helfried at the ritual grounds in the afternoon.

Until then, I proceeded as planned. While conducting practical tests of magic tools, I continued constructing the public bathhouse. Since everyone wanted to see the construction process, I moved around with them while building various parts.

Now then. The public bathhouse would be quite a large facility overall. Following the design model, I created waterways underground and prepared the facility to draw hot water to various locations.

For manipulating water flow and generating bubbles, I used panel-type and pipe-type magic tools. They had a simple structure that allowed water they touched to flow with arbitrary force and direction.

By placing these in the walls and floors of baths and pools, I could draw water to desired locations, create flows, or even recreate jacuzzis.

Some parts weren’t ready for magic tools yet, so in those cases I stopped at the stage before incorporating them, completing only the preliminary preparations.

I had golems carry materials from the nearby storage area. I enclosed the site with walls and built an entrance gate.

This area was planned to have facilities like an admission counter, facility guidance, baggage storage, and a shop selling bathrobes.

From the lobby, through a corridor, to a separate two-story building. This was planned to be the hot spring facility.

Separate large baths for men and women with a dining hall, a rest area and terrace on the second floor, plus a game room. Furthermore, I created a slide on the rooftop for people to slide down from there.

The first-floor large bath would have regular bathtubs, a waterfall bath, jacuzzi-style baths, and a sauna. The second-floor terrace would have a foot bath.

I filled the jacuzzi with water and actually operated the magic tools. I conducted tests while checking things like whether the water pressure was appropriate. Marlene was staring intently at the jacuzzi.

“Once it’s finished, shall we all get in together?”

When I said this, Marlene looked up and nodded with a cheerful smile. I thought it would be good to have everyone serve as monitors too.

Moving to the rooftop. I prepared three slides. They would run parallel while winding, leading to the pool at the end. I installed stairs beside the pool so people could go to the rooftop without passing through the building.

“It’s much larger than the one at the lake, isn’t it?”

Grace looked down at the slides from the rooftop and spoke.

“This one isn’t makeshift.”

“I’m more surprised that you made something like that on the spot…”

“Well, um…”

I returned an ambiguous smile to Alfred.
