I drew water using magic tools to the top of the slides, making it flow downward from the entrance. Just like with the jacuzzi, I adjusted things here while checking whether the water volume and force were appropriate.

I wanted to properly adjust the slides. By making aqua golems slide at significantly higher speeds than normal, I identified areas where there was danger of going off course.

“Here, it might be better to reinforce this.”

“Understood.”

I set up scaffolding at various points and carefully inspected the slides with Seraphina. I reinforced structurally weak sections. Later I would install safety nets to prevent falling accidents. Well, this should be sufficient for the hot spring facility and slides.

Next, the outdoor area. The outdoor facilities would be a shared space for both genders. While users would need to wear swimsuits or bathrobes—since swimsuits were high-quality items made from expensive materials and limited in number, I planned to sell affordable bathrobes instead.

Beside the slides, there would be a warm water pool and lazy river pool. To match the shallow children’s pool, I prepared small slides. I made the lazy river pool relatively shallow while checking the flow strength.

I installed a watchtower to oversee the entire pool facility. The watchtower would be staffed with personnel serving as lifeguards in case guests drowned in the pools.

To ensure they could rush to any discovery immediately, I added doors that could be opened to jump out from the watchtower. They would wear aerial combat gear and head directly there. They would rescue drowning people using magic tools for underwater breathing.

Taking the opportunity, I had Sheila test the usability of the watchtower.

“I’ll give it a try.”

Sheila opened the door, jumped out from the watchtower, and glided through the air to the other side of the pool. Then she turned back toward us and waved. Irmhild smiled and waved back from the top of the watchtower.

Hmm. The usability doesn’t seem bad. While they need to get used to the aerial combat gear, if they think of it as part of rescue training, it shouldn’t be a problem.

Continuing with the public bathhouse construction in this manner, it reached a reasonably good timing.

After heading to the ritual grounds, having lunch, and relaxing in the gazebo, Prince Helfried arrived by carriage.

“Good afternoon. It’s been a while.”

“Long time no see.”

I returned the greeting to Prince Helfried, who had gotten off the carriage and bowed.

“I heard you were creating this district and buildings, Ambassador. I never imagined you’d even build the outer walls…”

Prince Helfried looked around at the surroundings with wide eyes.

“The townscape is still incomplete, so it’s rather bleak.”

“Not at all. I’m astonished. I apologize for making such a request when you’re so busy.”

“Not at all. Working continuously would be exhausting.”

“I’m relieved to hear you say that.”

After exchanging brief greetings, I showed him to the reception room in the ritual grounds’ accommodation facilities and decided to listen to what he had to say along with Rosemary.

“Long time no see, Helfried.”

“Sister… it’s been a while.”

When Rosemary entered the room and spoke to him, Helfried straightened his posture. Perhaps due to previous circumstances, he seemed somewhat nervous. Well, that can’t be helped.

When I told Rosemary that Helfried wanted to meet, she said she would go easy this time. Since the situation has changed, Rosemary also has fewer reasons to particularly keep Helfried at a distance.

“Your Highness Helfried, is your business still concerning your sister, Lady Rosemary?”

“Yes. Father has told me certain things. That’s precisely why I’m worried, so to speak. I understand it’s probably unreasonable for me to be concerned about such things… but I was shocked when I heard she had been moved.”

King Melvin’s explanation had apparently obscured the specific core details, such as the magic potion and disguising as a fortune teller.

However, he had apparently explained to Prince Helfried the part about Rosemary being involved in schemes related to royal succession, holding nobles’ secrets, and using them for blackmail.

So the explanation had also been given that she was imprisoned in the northern tower as punishment for that.

Imprisonment could also be viewed as isolation to prevent assassination or retaliation. Prince Helfried should understand that much.

But currently, Rosemary is out here like this. From Prince Helfried’s perspective, he must be worried about dangers like assassination.

In that case, I should start with reporting Rosemary’s current situation. It would probably help him understand if I explained why I’m taking care of her.

“Actually, Lady Rosemary has been helping me with deciphering ancient documents related to labyrinths for some time now.”

“Sister deciphering ancient documents…?”

“Yes. She has talent in magic. It might be close to His Majesty’s intention to impose labor as atonement during her imprisonment.”

“I also understand Father’s intentions that way. Well, deciphering ancient documents wasn’t painful enough to be called atonement. I’ve been enjoying it reasonably well.”

She said this while shrugging her shoulders.

Explaining it as helping with deciphering labyrinth-related ancient documents as part of my work as the Otherworld Ambassador shouldn’t be problematic.

“But a problem arose. Actually, among those ancient documents, some contained magical traps. Things like books that drag souls inside.”

I also revealed that during that incident, Rosemary’s life was endangered by a magical trap set by an ancient magician. I couldn’t explain why Rosemary is with me without mentioning that part.

“I fell into that trap—and Theodore chased after me into the book and saved my life. I consider it an irrepayable debt.”

Rosemary closed her eyes, and Prince Helfried looked genuinely surprised.

“We’ve also learned that such magical traps can be countered particularly with strong Moon Goddess’s Blessing.”

“Ah, so if Marlene were here…”

Helfried seemed to understand. While I needed to keep Claudia’s matter secret, he had probably heard about Marlene’s marriage arrangement and knew about her talent as a shrine maiden.

“Yes. So to protect herself from magical traps, she’s progressing with ancient document deciphering at home. As assassination countermeasures, she’s also using disguise with rings.”

As a member of Verdgar’s royal family, he should know about disguise rings. Revealing this shouldn’t be problematic either.

“That’s why, unlike when I was imprisoned, I can go out like this. This must also be Father’s mercy. Does that satisfy your concerns?”

“Yes. Various things make sense now. The rumors about you, Ambassador… from what I’ve heard, they’re all quite extraordinary, so this might actually be the safest place in Termwills.”

What kind of rumors… well, I won’t ask. They probably have strange exaggerations attached.

“Um… for me, there’s just one more thing I’d like to ask… or rather, something that’s been on my mind.”

“What is it?”

When I asked, Prince Helfried seemed to hesitate for a moment, but after taking a deep breath, he broached the subject with a serious expression.

“—Sister’s marriage prospects.”

+++

# **238 – Sister and Brother**

“That’s quite an interesting story, Helfried.”

Rosemary spread her feather fan and smiled as she covered her mouth. Though she was smiling, she clearly wasn’t pleased with Helfried’s words. That was the impression I got.

“However, even without you telling me such things, I intend to do as I please—”

“That’s impossible.”

Helfried didn’t back down from Rosemary. He cut her off as if interrupting her words.

Perhaps his reaction was unexpected, as Rosemary’s eyes widened while she still covered her mouth with her feather fan.

“The sister I knew in the past might have ignored Father’s wishes and done as she pleased. But that’s impossible now. Even I can understand that. Father wouldn’t actively pursue marriage negotiations for a sister who carries the risk of conflict with other nobles.”

Helfried spoke these words to Rosemary with an air of indifference. Somehow… it gave me the impression that after being thoroughly defeated last time, he had become defiant.

But indeed. When it comes to Rosemary, there’s the danger of assassination, and the possibility of her information being exploited.

Considering the connections Rosemary had built, depending on who she married, it could significantly affect the balance of power.

But telling me this here… In Helfried’s thinking, he probably wanted me to consider it. To ensure my sister’s position remains stable going forward, he likely wants me to take some normal initiative.

“I’m sure you’d say it’s none of my business, sister. But you know, something you said earlier made me wonder. Once you finish deciphering the Ancient Document, are you planning to return to the North Tower?”

“You…”

At Helfried’s words, Rosemary furrowed her brow.

“You’re going to accept that too, right? Even I can read your thinking to some extent. I am your brother, after all.”

“Fine by me. That place isn’t so bad either.”

“There you go again. Wasn’t it you, sister, who told me before to consider if there’s a path forward before giving in to despair or acting rashly?”

Rosemary was at a loss for words in response. Perhaps she realized she was responding to provocation with provocation.

Helfried turned to me and bowed his head.

“I’m sorry. For suddenly bringing up such a topic. I know it’s rude. I just don’t want to see my sister return to that tower.”

…I see. Now I understand. King Melvin, given the circumstances, probably can’t broach this subject with me himself, and Helfried, having heard about the situation, likely thought this far based on his experience with his sister’s behavior.

“If that’s the case… I think my fiancées should be here for this conversation.”

If we’re going to discuss this further, everyone should be present. I don’t want to proceed with such matters without informing them.

“That won’t be necessary. While they are indeed involved parties, if this is about confirming feelings, it should be settled once I state my feelings first, shouldn’t it?”

“…No matter the circumstances, I can’t imagine you would trouble yourself with someone you dislike.”

“Be quiet. I’ll admit I’m fond of him, but I don’t particularly like Theodore in that way—”

She stood up, thrusting her feather fan toward Helfried.

Just as she spoke those words, Rosemary’s voice stopped. Then she shook her head.

“…If I were to say this outright, it would probably violate it. …Yes, that’s right. I admit it. It’s exactly as you imagine.”

Violate—the Oath Magic, I suppose. Once activated, there’s no point in denying it with words, and more than anything, she probably disliked breaking a vow she imposed on herself more than revealing her true feelings.

Probably, when questioned about such feelings, she considered continuing to deny them while interacting with me as betrayal. That’s likely how Rosemary perceived it.

We decided to continue the conversation after having Grace and the others join us.

About Rosemary’s future plans. Once matters related to the Demon are resolved, Rosemary, having lost her reason to stay, might have intended to return to the North Tower. That would indeed be very characteristic of Rosemary’s way of thinking.

Even King Melvin, while probably not sending her back to the North Tower, would still need to restrict Rosemary’s movements to some extent due to the knowledge she possesses.

“…I’ve lived in different places and with different perspectives than Grace and the others. As someone whose life was saved by Theodore—I can’t possibly say something like ‘because I was forgiven.’ Even if we could fight together, I’m not suitable to stand by your side. It’s a separate issue from feelings.”

Saying this, Rosemary shrugged her shoulders.

“We too… have certainly been concerned about Rosemary-sama’s position.”

Grace spoke after hearing the story.

“It’s true that for us as well, there were many aspects of Rosemary-sama that couldn’t be seen through rumors alone.”

“Yes. But we had time.”

Ashley continued the words, and Grace nodded.

There certainly are aspects of Rosemary’s personality and inner thoughts that are difficult to gauge. Rosemary undoubtedly desired the throne and didn’t hesitate in her methods, and everyone knows that. The rumors circulating in society are also varied.

“I believe we’ve already been given sufficient time to be certain we can trust you.”

Time. The time spent together. Sleeping under the same roof, standing shoulder to shoulder as we headed to the Labyrinth, fighting Demons. And how we felt about Rosemary through all that.

Claudia spoke.

“When I reflect on my own situation, I have thoughts about being returned to a position close to confinement. But even setting that aside, I don’t think there’s any reason why you wouldn’t be suitable.”

“Since coming here, Marie sister has seemed much happier than when she was at the Castle. I like sister as she is now.”

Marlene took Rosemary’s hand.

“Sister… I—”

Rosemary showed a slightly surprised expression before smiling self-deprecatingly and looking down.

“…You know. I felt that Marie’s previous way of living had some similarities to mine. Though our positions and goals were different.”

We had clashed due to conflicting interests, but building her own foundation through her own power, changing her surroundings to make her life easier—in that aspect alone, she was the same as me. In Rosemary’s case, the inherent element of being royalty was mixed in, with responsibilities and pride attached from the beginning, I think.

Considering that and putting myself in Rosemary’s position…

Whether it’s confinement or seclusion, if it were me, I think it would be painful. I absolutely detest living with constrained feelings.

Even so, Rosemary, perhaps because of the pride of being born royalty, wouldn’t accept being with me without a proper justification.

“If you say you’ll return when you lose your reason, then we just need to create that reason.”

Saying this, I reached out my hand toward Rosemary.

Rosemary’s eyes widened, and after looking between my hand and my face, she spoke.

“…If I’m with you, you’ll probably have difficulties? My position as an outcast won’t change, and my personality is twisted like this, you know.”

“That’s exactly why. If I disliked you, I wouldn’t invite you to my home even with a reason.”

When I answered, Rosemary smiled wryly and hesitantly took my hand. Grace and the others smiled.

“Congratulations.”

After witnessing this, Helfried spoke, and Rosemary turned her head toward him with an unhappy expression.

“Helfried. You remember this, right?”

“Ahaha. I’ll be returning to my study abroad soon anyway, so revenge won’t come for quite a while, I think.”

“Really…”

Rosemary shook her head, her cheeks reddening.

“…I’ll report to Father myself later.”

“That’s good. I’ll stop my meddling here.”

Saying this, Helfried laughed.

“Your Highness Helfried, how long do you plan to stay here?”

“I plan to remain in Termwills for a few more days.”

Hmm. A few more days, huh. Will it be in time for the planned opening date?

“We’re planning to gather related parties and close friends for the opening of the hot spring facility. What do you think?”

Once everything is complete, I thought we could invite acquaintances to enjoy the hot springs ahead of others.

Well… it will probably be quite a luxurious and chaotic gathering. The prime minister seemed quite looking forward to it too, so should I invite him? If it’s through King Melvin’s inquiry, he probably wouldn’t feel hesitant.

“Can I attend too?”

“Yes. You’re welcome.”

When I answered, Helfried smiled happily, and Rosemary shrugged her shoulders. From this reaction, it’s somewhat unclear how Rosemary truly feels about Helfried being invited.

Well then. A few more days, huh. I need to work hard to ensure there are no issues with the hot spring facilities.

+++

# **239 – New System**

I headed to the Royal Castle with Marie—that is, Rosemary in disguise. Although the report was to be given by Rosemary, it wouldn’t do for me not to be present.

We met with King Melvin in the salon and recounted the events that had transpired.

“…I see. So it was Helfried.”

King Melvin closed his eyes and murmured as if to himself.

“However, this matter will be meaningless without my father’s approval.”

At Rosemary’s words, King Melvin nodded and turned to face me.

“Theodore. You and Rosemary… are you truly fine with this?”

He looked directly into my eyes as he asked. It felt like he was both confirming and testing my resolve.

“There are no issues. I will take responsibility for everything that has happened up until now, and everything that will happen from now on.”

I answered clearly while looking at King Melvin, and he nodded.

“Very well. When it comes to Rosemary’s current situation, the root cause lies partly in my own negligence. Though I have entrusted her to you, I will not hesitate to offer my assistance.”

“Thank you.”

When I bowed my head, King Melvin suddenly smiled, and a relaxed atmosphere filled the room.

“Still. Two members of the royal family marrying into the same household—that’s unprecedented, isn’t it?”

At Rosemary’s joking words, King Melvin gave a wry smile.

“Perhaps it is. However, it is commensurate with your achievements. But to speak plainly, as a parent, there is a part of me that feels relieved. Some may view this as a reward for you, but that is not how I see it.”

Well… the royal family was originally like relatives anyway. There might be various perspectives regarding Rosemary’s marriage, but the reality is different. I certainly heard King Melvin’s words. That was enough.

Now then. With five fiancées… the intervals between their turns to sleep beside me at night have become considerably longer.

So, we discussed the future among myself and the girls, and decided on arrangements—or rather, a new system. We would begin implementing it starting today.

I absolutely must properly address Grace’s blood-sucking reaction relief and perform Circulating Ki for Ashley and Claudia. There’s also the aspect of treating my fiancées as equally as possible.

Therefore, after returning home and having dinner, two people would be on either side of me in the Japanese-style room. One person during bath time. Then, two people on either side in the bedroom before sleeping. By rotating one person at a time in each location, everyone would get sufficient time at least once.

Since it was Rosemary’s first day, she would join me at bedtime, so first, I spent time interacting with Marlene and Claudia together in the Japanese-style room.

Claudia sat close beside me, while Marlene was in a position where I could hold her. Marlene was originally a Shrine Maiden apprentice. The two of them get along well. Marlene was in quite a good mood.

“Hehe…”

Claudia stroked Marlene’s hair, and Marlene smiled back at her. The way they smiled at each other made them look like close sisters, but at times like these, Claudia sometimes revealed an expression befitting her accumulated years. In other words… a smile similar to Mother’s… So, rather than sisters, they gave the impression of mother and daughter.

I included Marlene in Claudia’s Circulating Ki, and the three of us circulated our Magical Power. Both of their bodies were small and slender, and even when they leaned their weight on me, it wasn’t heavy at all.

Marlene, who had been looking at me, seemed to notice something and tugged lightly on Claudia’s sleeve.

“Hm? What is it, Marlene?”

Following Marlene’s pointing finger, Claudia let out an understanding “Ah.” What Marlene had indicated seemed to be around my ears.

Marlene stood up and brought an ear pick.

“Hmm. I see.”

“That’s right. Shall we do it together then? Theodore, would you rest your head on my lap?”

Marlene nodded repeatedly at Claudia’s words. Claudia patted her own lap. Following their suggestion, I laid my head on Claudia’s thigh.

Receiving a lap pillow from Claudia, I had my ears cleaned slowly.

“Does it hurt?”

“…It’s fine. The pressure is just right.”

Claudia carefully cleaned my ears with the same calm smile she had shown Marlene. Marlene, lying down beside us, had an innocent smile and gently blew on the cleaned ear to make it even cleaner. It was unbearably ticklish.

“Ah. I remembered something.”

Irmhild, who had been watching the scene, spoke.

“Hm, what?”

“That I might have been put to sleep by Claudia-sama before. Memories from when I was little are very hazy, though.”

“I did take care of small children in the Labyrinth Village too.”

I see. Well, regarding her background as a goddess… The reason Claudia’s smile reminds me of Mother’s probably stems from that aspect.

I spent a relaxing time with Marlene and Claudia until bath time.

And then, bath time. I hadn’t intervened regarding the order, but it seemed Ashley would be first to join me.

“Excuse me.”

Ashley, who entered the bathroom… wasn’t in swimwear but was wearing white garments.

They were the clothes used by the Shrine Maidens and Clerics of the Moon Temple during their spiritual training Water Rituals. I was wearing the Cleric version. Ashley was wearing the Shrine Maiden training garments.

When we were searching for potential candidates for bathrobes to use at the hot spring facility, a Shrine Maiden stationed at the ritual grounds had suggested these as an option. We had them lend us enough for the Party Members.

To describe their shape, the Shrine Maiden version was like a one-piece that exposed the shoulders and back. It was close to the garments worn by women in ancient Greece. That was called… a chiton, I believe? Well… it’s a white garment that gives a pure impression. I think it suits Ashley well.

If they had been convenient to use, we would have adopted them as they were, but the hem was slightly too long, making them unsuitable for swimming, so we would have to work on the shape a bit more for them to serve as bathrobes.

The official bathrobes to be sold at the hot spring were ordered to be in a form like culotte skirts with gathered hems. What Ashley was wearing now was exactly the same as the garments used by the Temple Shrine Maidens.

“Then, I’ll wash your back.”

Ashley lathered up the Savona Tree soap with a washcloth and slowly scrubbed my back.

“After you’re done, I’ll wash your back too, Ashley.”

“Thank you. Then, I’ll be in your care.”

Just as Ashley had done for me, I washed her back with the washcloth.

“And then, um… I’ll wash your body.”

Ashley said, looking somewhat embarrassed.

“Then, I’ll wash my hair in the meantime… and after that’s done, I’ll be soaking in the bath.”

“Yes…”

Ashley nodded, her cheeks reddening. I washed my hair with the shampoo made from Savona Tree sap, thoroughly washed my body, and then got into the bath. After a while, Ashley entered the bath as well.

“Sorry to keep you waiting.”

Ashley walked through the bath and came close to my side.

…Since the Shrine Maiden training garments are white, when they get wet, they create quite a stimulating sight… but well, that’s part of it being training wear, I suppose. Areas like the chest apparently have double layers of cloth, so they’re reasonably well protected.

Even so, areas like the thighs had the cloth clinging tightly, revealing the skin tone beneath the garment… Hmm. I better not think about it too much.

“Then, come here.”

“Yes.”

I drew Ashley close to my chest in the bath and performed Circulating Ki. She let out a small, contented sigh. When I closed my eyes, she wrapped her arms around my shoulders and leaned her body against me.

I ran my fingers through her wet hair and gently stroked her cheek.

“Mmm…”

As I continued the Circulating Ki, Ashley, perhaps due to the comfort and the warmth of the bath, began to breathe softly as if falling asleep. Since we had set the bath to a lukewarm temperature to allow more time, she probably wouldn’t get overheated, but I’ve heard it’s not good to sleep in the bath.

Ashley also often stays up late studying noble etiquette and Magic, accompanying me in deciphering codes while working hard on her own studies. With training and Labyrinth Exploration too, she might be tired.

“Ashley?”

“Mmm… Ah, I’m sorry. Was I asleep?”

When I called out softly, she opened her eyes slightly.

“Are you a little tired?”

“No… It’s just that when you perform Circulating Ki on me, Theodore-sama, I feel incredibly at ease. So when I closed my eyes, I started to doze off. It’s like it reminds me of when I was little…”

“…I see.”

I returned a smile to Ashley. With five people, bath time is one person each now… Hmm. Let’s take our time and perform Circulating Ki.

After finishing my bath with Ashley, I left the bathroom. Until it was time to sleep in the master bedroom, everyone spent their time as they wished. In my case, I continued deciphering Mother’s notes. Playing cards is fine too, or spending time on embroidery or studies. Although my hands are occupied, it’s also time for everyone to spend as they please.

“…Right then.”

I stretched lightly and stood up.

“Are you retiring for the night?”

“Yeah. I’m starting to get sleepy.”

Grace asked. For sleeping tonight, Grace and Rosemary would be the ones on either side of me.

The bed was becoming rather cramped for six people to sleep in. So, I had used Wood Magic to modify it into a larger size, so now it’s designed to allow everyone to lie down and sleep comfortably.

“Mmm. Well then, it’s about time for us to return to our rooms too.”

Sheila said. It seemed they had been enjoying cards with Claudia, Irmhild, and Seraphina.

“Good night, Theodore.”

Said Seraphina.

“Yeah. Good night.”

“Good night.”

“Good night.”

Sheila, Irmhild, and Seraphina left the room.

I lay down on the bed. Everyone else came onto the bed as well. Everyone in their nightwear is quite a feast for the eyes. Since it’s after bathing, the scents of soap and shampoo tickle my nostrils.

Ashley and Claudia lay on either side of Marlene. Marlene, surrounded by Ashley and Claudia, looked very happy.

…And so, naturally, that meant Grace and Rosemary would be lying beside me.

“Somehow, this is… Sharing a bed with someone feels strange… Was it to address the reactionary resolution and perform Circulating Ki that we started this?”

Rosemary in her negligee seemed somewhat unsettled.

“Well, yeah.”

“You’ll find it enjoyable once you get used to it.”

Grace chuckled softly and gently rested her cheek against my shoulder.

“…Is that so?”

Seeing that, Rosemary also moved closer.

Perhaps because they’re the two older ones… the stimulation is quite strong in various ways. Rosemary has a good figure, but Grace has also… grown larger compared to last year. I won’t say in what, though.

Feeling such soft sensations on both sides, I turned off the lights. When I started the Circulating Ki, Rosemary beside me trembled slightly. Her heartbeat seemed to have quickened just a bit.

While sleeping, Rosemary shifted, and her hand touched mine. Rosemary’s body reacted slightly. I gently held her hand, and Rosemary didn’t pull away.

Like this, with Grace and Rosemary. Together, I’ll continue the Circulating Ki until we fall asleep.

The warmth and softness on both sides would keep me awake if I focused on them, so I decided not to think about it too much. That’s right… The hot spring. I’ll think about the hot spring.

Anyway. Soon, all the Magic Tools will be gathered, and the hot spring preparations will be complete. Then, finally, it will be time for the unveiling. I need to properly think about the greeting speech and arrangements.

+++

# **240 – A Thousand Guests, A Million Arrivals**

We began preparations the night before, heading out early in the morning to arrange dishes in the dining hall and advance the preparations for the grand opening.

That said, we had plenty of hands. This time, chefs had been dispatched from the Royal Castle, and the residents of Labyrinth Village also helped with the preparations. I was operating the Aqua Golems myself, so things went smoothly.

In the kitchen, the chefs were bustling about. White bread heaped in baskets. Platters of herb-stuffed poultry and meat pies, stew bubbling noisily in pots, fresh salads and fruit assortments. Elaborate candy sculptures… Various dishes were being prepared.

“Is this the right place to set up the Magic Tools?”

“Yes. They said if we line them up in the kitchen, they’ll handle the rest.”

The equipment for carbonated drinks, shaved ice, cotton candy, and more were also ready. Since those Magic Tools had also been delivered to the Royal Castle, the chefs were quite familiar with handling them.

So, rather than the kitchen, I focused my efforts on checking various minor details, like whether there were any deficiencies on the facility side. After all, the grounds were vast. Seraphina, Caduceus, and I split up to check everything.

“If you find any issues with structural strength, let me know immediately.”

“Okay. But everything seems fine for now.”

Seraphina smiled.

Well, then. The area around the pool drainage still required caution. This was a part prone to accidents. Using Aqua Golems, I had to meticulously check every nook and cranny. We had been repeating checks and Magic Tool operation tests for several days in a row.

The drain outlets were blocked with grates to prevent accidents… but just in case someone’s limb got sucked into a hole, I had also embedded a Magic Tool as a precaution.

If someone touching the Magic Tool embedded near the drain inlet sensed danger—it was designed to respond to that intent. The mechanism was such that the Magic Tool would activate, temporarily reversing the water flow to expel the person.

Operation check. No issues.

While I was going around checking here and there, time flew by. At the right moment, I went to the Gate to bring everyone over.

“Oh, Theodore.”

“Long time no see. I’m looking forward to enjoying myself today.”

“Hello, Theodore-san.”

From the Adventurer Guild: Guild Master Auria, Vice-Commander Oswald, and receptionist Heather.

“Theo-kun, I heard you built a hot spring town this time?”

“As always, the things you do are beyond the norm, huh?”

So said Forestbird’s Lucian and Robin. Fitz and Monica also smiled and greeted me. Along with those four, Siren Justia and Harpy Dominique had come as well.

“I’ve been looking forward to this ever since I received the invitation.”

“It was fun when we went to the sea before, too.”

“Both of you, please enjoy yourselves today.”

Irmhild was talking to Justia and Dominique.

So, just from the Adventurer Guild-related people, that was the lineup. Moreover, given the proximity, Penelope and the shrine maidens of the Moon Temple seemed to have come along as well.

“Thank you very much for inviting us today, Theodore-sama.”

At that point, I also bowed and returned the greeting.

“Likewise. Thank you for coming today.”

Marlene, with a happy expression, trotted over to Penelope, accompanied by Claudia. Penelope caught Marlene and smiled.

“It’s been a while, Claudia-sama. Marlene-sama, and everyone else, you all seem well.”

“Yes. Penelope, you look well too.”

Claudia returned a smile to Penelope.

With that, I guided them to the table for the Adventurer Guild-related personnel.

“Smells delicious, huh.”

Fitz reacted to the aroma of food wafting through the dining hall.

“Today, the Royal Castle’s chefs are showing off their skills.”

“That’s amazing.”

“Personally, I like Grace-san’s cooking too, though.”

“Indeed. I agree with that.”

Auria nodded in agreement with Monica’s comment.

Yeah, that’s right. When Grace was once invited by King Melvin, she thoroughly absorbed techniques from the Royal Castle’s cuisine.

“Today, the chefs have prepared everything so you can eat whenever you like. We’ll serve drinks first… but since there are places to swim within the grounds, if you plan to use those, it might be better to eat afterward.”

“Oh? That sounds interesting.”

Oswald reacted. Well, Oswald would be interested in that sort of thing, I suppose.

“We’ll also take time later to explain the facilities. Please enjoy conversing for now.”

With that, after a brief greeting to the Adventurer Guild members, I returned to the entrance gate to welcome the invited guests.

Next to arrive were Alfred, blacksmith Viola, Talcott and Cindy, Labyrinth Trading Company’s Miriam, and the Dwarf craftsmen employed by the company. These were the people related to the workshop and the Labyrinth Trading Company. Ophelia was also accompanying them today.

“Good work, Theo-kun.”

“Yeah. Good work. Did you sleep well last night?”

“Mm, well, sort of. I did wrap up a bit early, after all.”

Alfred gave a wry smile.

The Magic Tools for the hot springs were all assembled, but the armor wasn’t finished yet, so he was working hard. He said he wanted to finish it before we leave Termwills…

“No, even the entrance decorations are so detailed… I knew you were using Magic Construction, but… I feel your skills have improved since before.”

Miriam said this while looking around everywhere. Miriam seemed to be in quite high spirits, probably because she could see all sorts of rare things. Even though she was related to the workshop and could come see it if she wanted, it seemed she had waited patiently until completion.

Then Rosetta also peeked in.

“Hello, Theodore-kun. I hope you’re well.”

“Yes. Thanks to you.”

“Hello, Professor.”

“Ah, Ashley. Ophelia too.”

“It’s been a long time, Rosetta-sama.”

Noticing Rosetta, Ashley and Ophelia approached with smiles.

“You both look well.”

“Yes. Ashley-sama… I heard you fought a Demon again. I’m glad to see you don’t seem injured.”

“Thank you. My role isn’t one that puts me on the front lines much, though.”

“Is that so? What is it actually like, fighting a Demon?”

“Since Theodore-sama is with me.”

Ashley answered with an unburdened smile, and Ophelia giggled.

“I’ve brought them.”

“Good work, Sheila.”

Sheila also appeared at the entrance gate. She had guided Director Sandra of the West District Orphanage, then Brad and the other children, along with the staff members in charge. The orphanage folks were invited by me and King Melvin.

“It’s been a while.”

“Yes. It’s been a long time.”

Dorothy, the daughter of the former Thieves Guild Master, was also accompanying Sheila. She herself was Sheila’s friend and not a member of the Thieves Guild.

I had also reached out to Isabella, an executive of the Thieves Guild. I thought if we set aside positions and it was just personal… but she firmly declined, saying if people were coming from the Royal Castle, it would be better if she wasn’t here. Well, she laughed and said she’d go to the hot spring town privately another time, so not to worry…

“My, my… you’ve managed to gather quite the crowd, haven’t you?”

Rosemary gave a wry smile at the assembled faces.

“Indeed.”

Add to that Cecilia and Mihaela, who work at the house, the residents of Labyrinth Village, and then Spirit Tephra joining in—it’s a truly varied lineup.

I had also invited Gartner County and the Barony of Silun, but it seemed they couldn’t make it. I received a reply saying they’d come visit in early autumn.

As I ushered everyone into the dining hall and waited, timing it for when the invited guests were all assembled, King Melvin, Chancellor Howard, then Prince Josiah, Princess Stephania, and Prince Helfried appeared. Almost the entire royal family was present.

As escorts, Knight Order Commander Mildred and Court Magician Ricard. Furthermore, they were accompanied by royal guards. Mercedes and Chester were also invited from the Knight Order, but since the two were on vacation today, their participation wasn’t strictly in an official Knight Order capacity.

And on top of that, Marquis Zilbolt and his family were also accompanying them.

My, my. Even though I’m the one who invited them, this lineup… is quite something.

Everyone stood to welcome King Melvin. King Melvin, smiling, headed to the podium set up in a corner of the dining hall and began to speak.

“Everyone, well done. I am delighted that we have been able to welcome this auspicious day. I believe many of you already know, but most of this hot spring town is thanks to the blessings of Spirit Tephra, Otherworld Ambassador Theodore Gartner, and the people of Brightwelt Workshop. As you know, the Ambassador and the workshop were deeply involved in the establishment of the Boundary Theater as well. First, let us give unstinting praise and applause to these key players.”

King Melvin indicated me, Alfred, Viola, and Tephra, who were in the wings. Then, thunderous applause resounded throughout the dining hall. Alfred and I bowed properly in response. Tephra was smiling.

King Melvin said to me,

“Now then, Theodore. Let us have a word from you.”

“Thank you. Very well.”

I returned a smile to King Melvin’s informal words, bowed, and stepped onto the podium.

“Today, I have no words to express my gratitude for so many of you gathering here. I also extend my thanks to my friend, Magic Engineer Alfred, and for the cooperation of Spirit Tephra. From this day forward, I hope that the Fire Spirit Hot Spring will add modest enjoyment and color to the lives of those residing in Termwills, and that through the blessings of Spirit Tephra, daily life will become healthy and vibrant.”

After I gave my address, even louder applause erupted.

I bowed once more and passed the baton back to King Melvin.

“Indeed. If I speak too long, I will only keep everyone waiting unnecessarily. Now then, everyone, raise your glasses.”

Since it was for swimming and bathing, we avoided alcohol and made the toast with carbonated drinks. We raised our glasses in unison with King Melvin’s lead.

“Good work.”

When I returned to my seat after finishing the greetings, Grace said.

“Yeah. Well, these kinds of greetings make my shoulders a bit stiff, I guess.”

Saying that, I sat down.

“Fufu…”

Grace smiled happily.

“Hm? What is it?”

When I asked, Grace smiled somewhat shyly.

“No. How should I put it? When I think back to when we first arrived in Termwills, we only knew the Forestbird members, Rosetta-san… and then Heather-san, it feels quite poignant.”

“Ah…”

Yeah, that’s right. In the past, I think I caused Grace a lot of worry because of me, and even though we were leaving the stifling County, I’m sure she wasn’t without anxiety about starting a new life in a land where she knew no one.

But the fact that Grace is happy like that… well. It makes me happy too.

Now then. After this, I have to guide everyone through the various facilities, explain how to use them, and also explain things like bathrobes. The schedule is to have everyone actually use the place after those explanations. I hope everyone likes it.

# **241 – Fire Spirit Hot Springs**

“For those who brought swimwear, that’s perfectly fine. For those who didn’t, please use these bathrobes. We ask that you wear these while inside the facility. We plan to sell them eventually, but for now, consider them complimentary samples.”

I distributed the prepared bathrobes to those without swimwear. Since the shrine maidens’ original water ritual garments were somewhat problematic with their sheer fabric, I had them dyed to address that issue.

The designs were relatively inoffensive—some had trunks-style bottoms, others had culotte-style skirts. They were fastened with a string around the waist, allowing some flexibility in sizing.

Once the bathrobes were distributed, we moved on as I explained each area, starting with the large bath.

When I led them to the men’s bath, exclamations of awe arose. The large bath, filled with steam and illuminated by sunlight, had an otherworldly atmosphere. It was designed with the image of a submerged ruin. Aside from the washing area, waterfall bath, and sauna, most of the space was occupied by the bathing pool.

There was little difference between the men’s and women’s baths in terms of the large bath area. The entire structure was made of stone, with floors retaining some roughness to prevent slipping, while the walls and ceiling had a smooth, marble-like texture.

Thick pillars supporting the ceiling rose directly from the bathing pool. In the center of the pool was a pedestal with a carved statue of a woman tilting a water jar. Hot spring water flowed endlessly from the jar, filling the pool.

“This is the men’s bath. The hot spring’s effects include healing burns and skin diseases. It’s also said to speed up wound recovery and keep the skin moisturized. It has medicinal properties, contains magical power, and seems effective for certain internal diseases when ingested.”

The information about the spring’s effects was borrowed from Marquis Zilbolt. Hearing that it was highly effective for beauty seemed to please the female attendees.

“Now, this way.”

I guided them to a corner of the bath, where a circular partitioned bathing area was located—a jacuzzi-style bath.

Given it was a public bath, it was designed to accommodate a reasonable number of people. It was relatively large for a jacuzzi.

“What’s this? It looks like magic stones are embedded along the edge.”

King Melvin tilted his head.

“Yes. When you touch this—”

I activated the magic tool by touching the magic stone, and the bath began churning violently with water currents and bubbles. I noticed several people widening their eyes and leaning forward.

“This uses water currents and bubbles to relax the body and enhance the blood circulation effects of the hot spring.”

“Oh ho. An interesting idea.”

We moved on.

Passing the washing area and going behind the partition wall, we reached the waterfall bath section, where water poured down from near the ceiling. It flowed from a lion-faced design.

“What’s this?”

“This is a waterfall bath. It uses the force of the falling water to relieve muscle stiffness. You can use it by directing the flow onto your shoulders or the back of your neck.”

“I see. Between this and the earlier bubble bath… it’s quite fascinating.”

It was Chancellor Howard who showed strong interest, staring intently at the lion’s face.

“Let’s move on. This way.”

Timing it right, I headed toward the sauna door. A water station and cold bath were prepared beside the entrance.

“This is the steam bath. Since the goal is to sweat, please drink water before entering. After sweating inside, you can tighten your skin in the cold bath.”

I explained how to use the sauna and its precautions.

Well, that should cover all the facilities in the large bath. Next, we moved to the second-floor relaxation area. Sofas and tables were placed here, allowing everyone to chat or relax as they pleased.

There was a counter where drinks could be served. A terrace overlooked the pool, complete with a foot bath. Next to the relaxation room was a game room. In terms of facilities, it was probably similar to the entertainment room in my house.

“It’s… incredibly thorough, isn’t it?”

Howard seemed astonished but gave a wry smile.

“There are still outdoor facilities as well. There’s also something on the rooftop here.”

I grinned, and Howard’s eyes widened.

“Ah… I was wondering about that.”

We moved to the rooftop. Everyone stared in amazement at the water slide.

“You slide down this.”

“Wow…!”

Brad from the orphanage, among others, had shining eyes.

“This looks fun!”

“Doesn’t it!”

I knew it would capture the interest of the orphanage children… but why were Auria and Miriam also sparkling with excitement?

“Monica, let’s try this later.”

“Sure, why not?”

“It’s quite high and scary, isn’t it?”

Forestbird and the others also seemed very interested. Well, the reaction isn’t bad.

“…Hmm. Is it safe?”

Howard asked while looking at the entire slide.

“We conducted repeated experiments to ensure you won’t fall off even at considerable speed—and we’ve installed nets so that even in the worst case, no one gets seriously injured.”

“I see…”

“As a precaution, please leave some interval between each slide, and once you slide down, move straight ahead immediately. This is to prevent users from colliding.”

I said this while looking at everyone’s faces. The orphanage children also nodded with serious expressions.

“And at the end of the slide… you can swim in that area.”

From the rooftop, I introduced the pools: the heated pool, the lazy river pool, and the shallow children’s pool. All were designed to be lit up at night for better visibility.

“That oval-shaped one over there has water flowing like a river. The current isn’t very fast… you can play by going with the flow or swim against it.”

“Oh ho.”

It was Oswald, the Vice-Commander of the Adventurer Guild, who reacted. He was talking to Chester about something. Probably planning to swim relentlessly against the current.

“If you want to play by going with the flow, use the outer circumference. If you want to swim against it, please use the inner circle.”

“Understood.”

“What’s that building in the middle?”

Penelope asked.

“That’s a watchtower to quickly spot anyone drowning.”

“As expected of Theodore-sama.”

Penelope smiled innocently and clasped her hands together.

“Well, that concludes my explanation and tour. I hope you all enjoy yourselves as you please.”

I bowed, and a round of applause broke out.

In any case, it was now free time. Everyone headed downstairs to change into their bathrobes. The orphanage children probably intended to come back to the slide after changing, so it was going to be hectic. They hurried downstairs… I think Auria was among them too.

“This is a more wonderful facility than I expected.”

“My, indeed it is.”

King Melvin, Chancellor Howard, and the rest of the royal castle group remained on the rooftop. The two laughed as they spoke.

“Facilities similar to this large bath are also prepared at the ritual site. Since that area is off-limits to non-related personnel, please use the lodging facilities at the ritual site for regular hot spring use.”

Specifically, the jacuzzi, waterfall bath, and sauna. Over there, wooden tubs are used, so you can enjoy the fragrance and ambiance of a cypress bath.

“Understood. But today is the unveiling of this facility, after all. I think I’ll enjoy this facility just like everyone else.”

“Yes.”

The people here today are all trustworthy individuals, so it should be fine.

“We too… well, let’s enjoy the bath first. Later, we can meet in the second-floor relaxation room or on the terrace.”

Saying this, King Melvin and the others also went downstairs.

“What about Grace and the others?”

“We were thinking of taking a bath first.”

They nodded in agreement. So, my party members are starting with the bath, it seems.

“Then I’ll start with the bath too.”

“Father mentioned meeting in the relaxation room later… so let’s meet there.”

Rosemary said.

“Sounds good. Everyone probably has things they want to do, like swimming, so is it alright if lunch is on your own?”

“That’s fine with us.”

For now, I’ll station Caduceus in the watchtower and have him monitor the poolside for safety.

The large bath is quite spacious. Even with the large number of people who came today, there’s still plenty of room.

“Ah, this is good. Really good.”

“I want this at home!”

“Can we buy it at the Labyrinth Trading Company?”

“Probably, the magic tools will be made-to-order, though.”

“Is that so! Well, just knowing it’s available is enough. It wouldn’t be bad to come here frequently.”

Chancellor Howard and Court Magician Ricard were operating the jacuzzi bath, laughing happily. Sitting across from them was the Dwarf master employed by the trading company… quite an unusual combination.

“Ah… nice water.”

Alfred let out a relaxed sigh. He seemed completely relaxed, leaning against the edge of the bath with his limbs sprawled out.

“…Well. Really, thank you for your hard work.”

Talcott and Cindy were there too, and so was Rosemary’s doll. We had more hands, but the workshop had its first major project in a long time.

“Talcott seems to have gone swimming, though.”

…Hmm. Talcott is currently in the lazy river pool with Oswald, Chester, Mildred, and Mercedes, swimming continuously against the current. He’s swimming at a pace like he’s in a race… but well, he must be enjoying himself in his own way.

The older children from the orphanage, the four members of Forestbird, and Auria, among others, seem to be repeatedly sliding down the water slide.

Penelope and Director Sandra are also near the children’s pool. They seem to be playing with the younger orphanage children. It’s like… a scene of kindergarten teachers leading their charges.

Well, the poolside is mostly peaceful like that. It’s best that everyone seems to be enjoying themselves.

“Ah, that’s right, Theo-kun. The dragon scale armor has turned out rather interesting.”

“Interesting how?”

“You gave me that fabric woven from Arachne thread before, right? I tried combining it with that. Then… it’s like a synergistic effect, I guess? The Arachne fabric seems to have become more fire-resistant.”

Oh ho. The strength of the Arachne thread was already quite high… and if it’s become more fire-resistant, we can expect some interesting effects.

“So, with that, I tried making armor by connecting dragon scales with Arachne thread. As ordered, it can be worn like clothing and covers a wider area with dragon scales. So I think the performance is better than expected.”

“That’s something to look forward to.”

“Well, if it’s not finished by the time we go to Marquis Zilbolt’s place… I was thinking maybe I could finish it while traveling to the Marquisate of Fobrester.”

Hmm. Well, Ophelia, the marquis’s daughter, is Albert’s fiancée. Later, when we go to the relaxation room, I’ll discuss it with King Melvin. Princess Stephania and Marquis Zilbolt were here too… It might not be a bad idea to have a relaxed meeting while soaking our feet in the foot bath on the terrace.

In any case, the hot spring facility seems well-received. I feel like it’s going quite well and I’m sensing a positive response. I think I’ll relax here a while longer, soaking in the bath and unwinding.

# **242 – Heading Towards Departure**

“Well now, the hot springs seem to be quite popular.”

“Truly, that’s wonderful. I was worried they might be too unconventional to be accepted.”

“That concern turned out to be unnecessary. I feel like a weight has been lifted from my shoulders.”

When I saw the Dwarves from the Labyrinth Trading Company holed up in the sauna competing over their endurance, I wondered what to do about it. Well, I suppose they enjoy it in their own way.

I placed hourglasses in the sauna. While endurance contests are fine, I made sure to instruct them to strictly adhere to the time limit measured by the hourglass when going outside… so it should be fine.

“Theodore.”

While relaxing with Alfred in the rest area, Sheila approached me, having just come out of the bath with Seraphina still perched between her cat ears. Irmhild, Dorothy, Justia, and Dominique were with her too.

“Hmm, what’s up?”

“Would it be alright if I took Dorothy and the others swimming?”

“Ah, yes. That’s fine. You should all go together. The children from the orphanage are playing there too.”

“Thank you for your consideration.”

Dorothy bowed her head politely.

“Not at all. Don’t worry about it. I’m happy if you can enjoy yourselves.”

After all, aside from us, Dorothy doesn’t have any acquaintances here. And even though we have a meeting with King Melvin, not everyone needs to stay in the rest area.

“Well then, we’ll be off for a bit.”

“Understood. What about the others?”

“We already discussed it in the bath.”

Hmm. So they’ve already coordinated.

“See you later then.”

“Mhm.”

“Yes.”

“We’re off.”

Seraphina waved along with everyone else from atop Sheila’s head. I waved back too and saw them off.

“Ah, Master, Lord Alfred too.”

“Good afternoon, both of you.”

Cecilia appeared at the entrance to the rest room as if crossing paths with them and bowed. Mihaela was with her.

“How was the bath?”

“It was excellent.”

“The design and decorations were also quite splendid.”

Mihaela smiled gently.

“Well, regarding the decorations, I referenced styles from books I borrowed from the academy, so I’m not very confident about them…”

I spent time staring at books, kneading Earth Magic, consulting with the female members, and progressing in that manner. Even though everyone’s aesthetic sense has improved, I still end up taking the lead on the details.

“The craftsmanship is intricate and truly wonderful.”

“I’m glad to hear you say that.”

“We’re back now.”

“Welcome back.”

“Oh, Al was with you too?”

Then Grace and the others arrived as well. Ophelia was accompanying them. Perhaps because they had just emerged from the hot springs, everyone’s skin had a reddish glow.

“Mmm, the breeze feels wonderful.”

Claudia closed her eyes contentedly as the wind from the terrace ruffled her hair.

“The terrace seats look nice and cool.”

Rosemary remarked while gently fanning herself with a feather fan. I think this might be the first time I’ve seen her actually using it for its intended purpose as a fan.

“Shall we move over there?”

“I’ll bring some drinks. Would you prefer them cold?”

Cecilia headed to the counter and brought carbonated drinks. We settled at the terrace table seats and decided to relax for a while.

“Hmm. Have I kept you waiting?”

While we were all relaxing on the terrace, King Melvin and his group arrived as well.

“Not at all. We were just chatting while waiting.”

“Hmm.”

“No, it’s a wonderful bath. I’m glad we came.”

“It felt like all our fatigue melted away in the water.”

Prince Josiah and Princess Stephania smiled.

Hmm. Both of them have duties as lords too. They’re probably quite busy.

Claudia was meeting Prince Josiah and Princess Stephania for the first time. I decided to introduce Claudia to the two of them first.

“Your Highness Josiah, Your Highness Stephania. This is Claudia.”

When I introduced her, both their eyes widened. This was also something King Melvin needed to discuss with them.

“We have heard about you from our father. It is an honor to meet you.”

“It is a pleasure to meet you, Lady Shuath.”

The two of them bowed to Claudia as subjects.

“There’s no need to be so formal. Nice to meet you.”

Just as the introductions with Claudia were completed, the members of the Zilbolt marquis household and Tephra also arrived at the rest room.

“All the necessary people are gathered. Then, let’s begin our discussion.”

At King Melvin’s words, we nodded and gathered around the table. Me and Claudia. King Melvin, Prince Josiah, and Princess Stephania. Along with Marquis Zilbolt and Tephra.

I used Wind Magic to cancel sound, taking measures to ensure our terrace conversation wouldn’t leak elsewhere.

“Now, the reason I’ve asked for your time is regarding the matter of the envoy to Silvatoria. The plan is to first go to the Marquisate of Fobrester. Then via the Marquisate of Zilbolt to the royal capital.”

“About that… I understand that Theodore-sama will be providing my escort?”

Princess Stephania inquired.

“Indeed. Theodore has agreed to cooperate.”

“That is, if it’s acceptable to Your Highness Stephania.”

Considering the matter with Roy, even if one understands logically, there might be reservations. Whatever Roy was truly thinking internally, outwardly he had behaved as a close brother.

So if she doesn’t want me to accompany her, then that’s that. Either Stephania’s escort would be someone else, or we would need to appoint someone other than Princess Stephania as the envoy.

“…Thank you. You’re kind.”

Princess Stephania closed her eyes and smiled faintly.

“But, let me say this clearly once more—you need not trouble yourself over it.”

As she said this, Princess Stephania looked somewhat lonely.

“That matter… Stephania and I surely share some blame too. It means we, who should have fulfilled our duties, were inadequate.”

At Prince Josiah’s words, King Melvin also nodded. We couldn’t delve too deeply into it in front of Marquis Zilbolt… but I silently bowed in response to their words.

“Personally, I don’t think I could ask for anyone better than you. So, please take care of me.”

Saying this, Princess Stephania extended her hand.

“Understood.”

When I shook her hand and nodded, Princess Stephania laughed.

“Hmm. So the envoy and escort are decided then.”

“Then we’ll also prepare for the journey according to the departure date.”

First, using the Dragon Palanquin to go to Marquis Fobrester’s territory. Then from there by sea to the Marquisate of Zilbolt.

The ship that Marquis Zilbolt arrived on to Termwills would be sent back directly to Silvatoria. However, neither Marquis Zilbolt nor the witch would be on that ship.

If the Crown Prince had come to welcome the witch, this could serve as a diversion tactic.

“Though my power is limited… I would like to offer my cooperation as well to ensure your activities in the royal capital proceed smoothly.”

Said Marquis Zilbolt. If Crown Prince Zadias was connected with demons, it could even pose an existential crisis for Silvatoria. Judging from the Marquis’s character and from the perspective of shared interests for personal safety, he should be trustworthy.

“Marquis, do you have a base in the royal capital?”

“Yes. I have a separate residence. Please feel free to use it if needed.”

“That would… be very helpful.”

It’s only natural that high-ranking nobles would have separate residences in the royal capital for their activities…

The Marquis has his Intelligence Unit including Elmer and Donovan, among others. Since we’d gain both a base and personnel, it’s reassuring. I think Elmer and the others are quite elite.

“Your Majesty. I would also like to request permission to accompany them as far as the Marquisate of Fobrester.”

Alfred said.

“Oh? Why is that?”

“To support the ambassador, you could say. There’s something I want to make and give to them before departure, but it seems I won’t quite make it in time.”

“Very well. Permission granted.”

Hmm. I suppose the arrangements are about set then.

When I looked from the terrace toward the poolside, I saw the contrasting—and somewhat indescribable—sight of Oswald, Chester, and other Knight Order members swimming against the current as usual… while nearby, rather than riding the current, Sheila was simply floating and being carried along by the water. The fact that Seraphina was still perched on her head made it all the more surreal.

The children from the Labyrinth Village and the orphanage were getting along well… the poolside was truly peaceful and harmonious.

…Seeing Auria and Miriam hitting it off and sliding down the waterslide together… well, I suppose I shouldn’t think too much about it. Miriam knows a lot of people, and they might have already been acquainted anyway.

+++

# **243 – Travel Preparations**

The hot spring facility’s grand opening was truly a success. I’ve heard talks about opening shops in the hot spring town have already begun, so development will likely progress rapidly from here.

King Melvin will be responsible for the management during our absence, keeping in mind the founding principles of establishments like the Boundary Theater and others.

As befits a public bathhouse, the admission fee is planned to be reasonably priced. Well, it’s part of civic entertainment and welfare benefits. My goals, Claudia’s wishes, and the safety of the Labyrinth Village residents—if all these align in direction, there’s nothing more to say.

With the hot spring town matters settled for now, we’re preparing for our journey to Silvatoria.

“Don’t we need drinking water?”

“We can create it with Life Magic when needed, so we should be fine. Just pack empty canteens.”

“Understood.”

Grace nodded, sorting necessary from unnecessary items, and loaded luggage into the dragon palanquin for our group—me, Claudia, and Seraphina. Seeing Lavigne supporting Seraphina from below as she struggled with a heavy bag was quite a heartwarming scene. Additionally, Tephra, who’s staying over at our house, is also helping with carrying the luggage.

Irmhild and Rosemary are organizing the loaded cargo, while Marlene and Sheila check against the list to ensure nothing is missing.

“What about the Potions?”

“They’re bulky, so let’s take a moderate amount. We plan to return via teleportation once we reach Mt. Tephra anyway.”

“Understood.”

Ashley transfers the Potions from small bottles into silver containers suitable for transport in the dragon palanquin.

The drawback of Potions is that overusing them in a short time can cause poisoning symptoms. Considering that both Ashley and I can use Healing Magic, in our Party they’re strictly supplementary.

While Magic Potions for magical power recovery are convenient, the replenished magical power takes a little time to settle in the body. The others can replenish consumed magical power through Circulating Ki, so we don’t need to carry too many.

“I see. So we can manage with minimal changes of clothes too.”

Rosemary remarked, noting the scarcity of clothing among the loaded luggage.

“Yeah. We might need dresses once we reach the royal capital, but we can collect those when we return once.”

“Ah. That combat dress suitable for that labyrinth?”

“Yes, that one.”

At my words, Rosemary grinned.

It’s a dress made from Lunaworm material, adorned with Magic Stone decorations, allowing multiple Enchantments like Protection. The last time I brought it out was probably when the previous Marquis Broderick invited us to a dinner.

It incorporates Aerial Combat Gear, includes anti-poison Magic Tools and an Amulet of Evil Repulsion, fully prepared against poisoning and Curse Magic… It’s no wonder Rosemary calls it a combat dress. Probably, Rosemary prefers that kind of Equipment.

“Mmm. All set.”

Sheila said, comparing the list I prepared with the luggage loaded into the dragon palanquin. Marlene also nodded seriously with a grave expression.

“Good. I’ll do a final check myself.”

Clothing, food, cooking utensils, tableware, seasonings, and other daily necessities. Blankets and Lanterns. Compass and map. Hobby items like cards, books, and musical instruments. Potions, anti-poison Magic Tools, etc.

Soap and shampoo made from Savona Tree sap. We plan to take a generous amount of these. Many of our female members have long hair, and hygiene management contributes to maintaining health.

Even so, I think the luggage is relatively light for our numbers. Besides Mt. Tephra, we can resupply in either the Marquisate of Fobrester or the Marquisate of Zilbolt.

“May I ride along as well?”

Tephra inquired. She probably means that teleporting ahead would free up space in the dragon palanquin, but… Claudia smiled and said,

“Traveling together doesn’t sound bad, does it? Even otherwise, we tend to be bound to our land, don’t we?”

“Hmm. Indeed.”

Tephra nodded with a solemn expression.

“That’s why preparing for the journey like this, all together, is very enjoyable.”

Saying that, Claudia showed a gentle smile.

Yeah, for Claudia, until now, she couldn’t even travel casually.

So surely, from her tone, this time is more precious than we might imagine. It was probably the same when we went cherry blossom viewing or visited the Count’s territory.

Perhaps Tephra also has thoughts about being bound to land, as she nodded quietly.

“Indeed. I always thought staying in the mountain I was born on was natural, but… I too am somewhat excited. That must be what it means.”

Tephra turned to me and spoke.

“So, I’ll be counting on you from now on as well. My friend.”

“Easy enough. You’re always welcome to visit us anytime.”

“Mmm.”

Tephra smiled happily. Then she turned to Claudia and said,

“Shall we increase small trips, not like this long journey? Like spring flower viewings.”

“Yes. That kind. Having a purpose makes it hectic; let’s make it pure recreation.”

“Lovely.”

Saying that, Claudia smiled joyfully.

Once the departure preparations are complete—all that’s left is to properly prepare for our absence.

I decided to gather Cecilia, Mihaela, and the main residents of the Labyrinth Village in the courtyard to discuss precautions.

“The Knight Order will increase patrols, but during our absence, ensure you can evacuate to the Labyrinth Village if problems arise.”

“Understood.”

At my words, Cecilia nodded with a serious expression.

Even when entrusting the house to others, having those with martial arts training like Cecilia and Mihaela in command puts me at ease. We know from the Thief gang attack that they have the courage to act in emergencies.

“Regular contact via Communication Devices, operation of Alarm Devices at night, and roll calls for Labyrinth Village residents. Just handle these areas thoroughly.”

Both Cecilia and Mihaela have been given Communication Devices, and Bracelets have been issued by Claudia to enable evacuation to the Labyrinth Village. If necessary, everyone can retreat to the Labyrinth Village.

Alarm Devices and a security system using simple Dolls made by Rosemary. Furthermore, the training of Labyrinth Village residents is progressing, and almost everyone in the house has acquired self-defense means.

Originally, Labyrinth Village residents exceed human average in physical strength or possess special abilities. With training, they’re becoming considerable combat forces. For example, Centaurs… are naturally skilled in mounted archery and lance combat.

Thus, our household’s combat strength and Defense are substantial. With the contact system via Communication Devices and Claudia’s teleportation, we can rush back if needed, so there should be no worries about what’s left behind.

“I try to stay with Cecilia in the mansion as much as possible. If visitors come, Cecilia and I can assess their character together, wouldn’t that work?”

Said Fortok, the Carbuncle leader. Carbuncles seem to understand people’s heart movements. They can hide even in pockets and have a track record.

“If you can avoid being seen, that should be fine.”

“Mmm. We’ll be careful enough about that.”

“Yeah. Also, I’ll teach everyone the Magic Shield spell. Those who can use Magic should practice aiming to use it without incantation, along with basic magical power control exercises.”

The relevant Labyrinth Village residents nodded. Claire the Arachne is one of them.

Whether one can use Magic depends on individual differences in magical aptitude. That’s the same for humans and monsters… but monsters often have more peculiar magical aptitudes than humans, even if they possess magical power. So even if I want to teach Magic, there are parts that can’t proceed uniformly.

Therefore, I identify those with magical aptitude likely to use Magic through Circulating Ki and have them start with Life Magic and basic magical power control exercises.

Anyway, Magic Shield has wide applications. Above all, it’s a defensive spell. Whether mastered or not greatly changes survival rates. If usable by a group, it’s immensely reassuring, and there’s no loss in learning it.

“I will advance self-defense training.”

“Please do.”

Mihaela bowed quietly.

That covers the precautions during our absence. From me, I’ll immediately convey the Magic Shield incantation. Having them repeat it, then it’s up to individual practice.

Departure is early tomorrow morning. Party Members plus Princess Stephania, Alfred and Viola, Ophelia, and from Marquis Zilbolt’s house, Tephra.

In a large dragon palanquin, first to Marquis Fobrester’s place. Though it’s a journey with a purpose, I want the travel itself to be enjoyable.

+++

# **244 – The Crown Prince's Military Officer**

Early morning—. The royal castle personnel and the Zilbolt marquis household were scheduled to meet at the royal castle.

The dragon palanquin loaded with luggage had already been left at the royal castle, so all that remained was for everyone to board the carriages and head toward the royal castle.

Cecilia and Mihaela, along with the residents of the Labyrinth Village, had gathered in the entrance hall to see us off.

“I’m off now, Cecilia-sama, Mihaela-sama.”

“Yes. Please take care, Grace-sama.”

“Grace-sama tends to push herself too hard when she’s being diligent. Please be careful.”

“Yes, Mihaela-sama.”

Grace smiled and nodded at their words. Farewells were exchanged all around.

“Don’t do anything reckless and get hurt.”

“Be careful, Irm.”

“Okay. I’m off now, Father, Mother.”

Irmhild exchanged hugs with her parents.

“Well then, Princess. Please take care.”

“Yes. I’m counting on everyone to look after things while I’m away.”

Fortok and the other labyrinth village residents were also holding Claudia’s hands and such.

After allowing sufficient time, I judged the moment right and spoke.

“Well then—I’m off.”

“Yes, my lord. Have a safe trip.”

“May fortune favor your arms.”

“Please leave matters here in our care. And please everyone, take care not to get injured.”

Cecilia and Mihaela saw us off with deep bows.

We boarded the carriage, smiled and waved at everyone, and they waved back.

“Good morning.”

“Morning, Viola.”

We picked up Viola along the way, who was carrying a large bundle, and continued on to the royal castle.

When we arrived at the royal castle, the dragon palanquins were already prepared in the square before the guesthouse. Two dragon palanquins. Since Elmer and the others would also be accompanying us via dragon palanquin, it had turned into a rather large formation.

The royal family including King Melvin, Ophelia, the knight order members, the three from the Zilbolt marquis household, and their retainers.

Penelope was there too. She had come to see us off.

“Good morning.”

“Hmm. It’s a fine morning worthy of a departure.”

King Melvin smiled. The sky was perfectly clear. It seemed we had been blessed with good weather.

“Good day to you, Ashley-sama.”

“Yes, Ophelia-sama.”

Ashley and Ophelia exchanged greetings. Perhaps because they interacted at the academy, the two seemed to be on good terms.

“Good morning, Marlene-sama. How are you feeling today?”

Marlene ran over to where Penelope was. Penelope gently caught Marlene as she smiled cheerfully, nodding as she stroked her hair.

“Sister. Please be careful.”

“You’re the one who should be careful. If you do anything unnecessary on my behalf, you’ll only invite trouble.”

“I’ll be careful.”

At Helfried’s words, Rosemary turned away with a sniff, still hiding her mouth behind her feather fan.

“Though you’ll be returning once… do take sufficient care.”

“Yes.”

I nodded at King Melvin’s words. After allowing ample time for farewells, we boarded the dragon palanquin harnessed to Lindwurm.

Though they were two large dragon palanquins, our palanquin would carry the two from the workshop, Ophelia, Princess Stephania, the Zilbolt marquis household, and Tephra. Quite a large party.

Once Elmer and the others had boarded the other dragon palanquin, I gave instructions to Lindwurm.

“Lindwurm. North. To the Marquisate of Fobrester.”

At my words, Lindwurm let out a cry. Spurred by Lindwurm’s voice, the wyverns all simultaneously beat their wings, and the dragon palanquin gained altitude.

Marlene waved from the window at King Melvin and the others below. King Melvin narrowed his eyes and waved back at Marlene—until eventually their figures grew increasingly distant and smaller.

The sparkling ocean bathed in sunlight was beautiful. The transparent sea viewed from high above in the dragon palanquin spread out below in shades of marine blue and emerald green.

The wyverns led by Lindwurm advanced above the coastal road. Continuing northeast like this would bring us to the Marquisate of Fobrester.

Irmhild began playing her lute. The refreshing, bright melody felt perfectly suited to the season and this scenery.

Alfred and Viola apparently intended to continue working during the journey. They were putting the finishing touches on clothing with dragon scales incorporated to protect vital areas.

It was protective clothing made of Arachne thread, with dragon scales sewn on as protectors covering key points. Though thin… apparently ordinary blades couldn’t even scratch it.

“Al must have it tough too.”

Ophelia peered at their work with a wry smile.

“I feel bad for keeping busy like this lately.”

“It’s quite alright. I don’t dislike seeing Al working, and it’s important work. Once we arrive at the territory and have time, we can talk leisurely.”

“Ahaha. Okay. I promise.”

At Alfred’s response, Ophelia smiled and nodded. Hmm.

Anyway, it would be bad to disturb them, so until Alfred’s work reached a stopping point, I should also handle what needed doing—like giving the marquis what I had for him and hearing what he had to say.

“Marquis. This is the witch’s bust.”

I presented a wooden box to Marquis Zilbolt.

It contained the bust of the witch Alvelinde and its casting mold.

“I have duly received it.”

Marquis Zilbolt accepted the wooden box, opened the lid to peer inside, and frowned slightly.

“My my… it’s the spitting image.”

“…Father… Is that really alright?”

The marquis’s daughter, Romina, asked anxiously upon hearing it was the witch’s bust.

“Though it’s the witch’s form, this is merely plaster. But it would be better if you didn’t look.”

The marquis smiled gently, closed the wooden box, and placed it in the corner of the dragon palanquin. Marquis Zilbolt had the air of a gentle, good father.

The marquis shifted his gaze to me and said.

“Ah, that’s right. Regarding the witch being a demon… there’s one person among the crown prince’s faction who concerns me.”

“Does that mean… you suspect that person of being a demon?”

At my question, Marquis Zilbolt shook his head.

“I don’t know. But his origins are unclear, you could say. He doesn’t seem connected to Silvatoria, and there are simply many mysteries about him. He’s a man whom the crown prince recommended four years ago, and who rapidly distinguished himself in the Magic Knight Order.”

Hmm. Since he’s mentioning this now, he must be someone worth being cautious about. Probably because he’s a military officer on the crown prince’s side, and if we happen to meet face-to-face, we should be careful.

“Would that be someone named Benedict?”

Princess Stephania inquired.

“Your Highness Stephania knew of him?”

“He’s famous in Silvatoria. I’ve never met him myself, but I’ve heard rumors at least.”

“What kind of person is he?”

“I hear he always wears a mask that covers his eyes.”

A mask… How eccentric.

“Conversely, you could say that’s his distinguishing feature.”

“Is that why he became famous?”

When I asked, Marquis Zilbolt gave a wry smile.

“I suppose that’s part of it. They say he himself claims it’s to hide burn scars on his face. Among the talents the crown prince has gathered, he’s the most mysterious, and a military officer with considerable skill in both martial arts and magic.”

“Any talk of him having bad conduct?”

“In that regard, he seems to be a person without problems.”

At Marquis Zilbolt’s words, Rosemary closed the feather fan she had been holding open and said.

“His origins are different. Meaning he has no connections or obligations to the royal palace or within the country, so the crown prince must find him useful.”

“Plus, if he has no bad reputation, that also means he has no grudges with anyone. For a crown prince who himself has a bad reputation, he might be easy to use.”

“There might be that aspect. Apparently he sometimes acts under direct orders from the crown prince himself. I thought there might be a chance we’d encounter him when he appears in the territory to fetch the witch, or when we’re pursuing the crown prince.”

I see… He told me because there’s a high likelihood we’d meet directly.

…Benedict, huh. While we can’t determine if he’s a demon… from what we’ve heard, at the very least he seems to be a direct subordinate of the crown prince?

Considering that the demon who infiltrated Termwills—Linette—was procuring a catalyst to pass through the barrier, timing-wise it wouldn’t be strange if this were a demon… maybe?

But having them run errands all over while making them use catalysts seems inefficient. Probably because those are precious items, demons can’t come in large numbers. Considering when he arrived in Silvatoria… it doesn’t seem related to the Sages’ Academy incident. Plus, there’s the question of how much he knows about the crown prince and serves him. I wonder what kind of person he really is.

“Not knowing his true face is problematic. We can’t assume he’ll keep his mask on when facing us.”

At Ashley’s words, Claudia nodded.

“That’s right. He might normally wear a mask for espionage purposes.”

That certainly seems plausible. Though hiding scars could also be a valid reason.

“I’ll keep it in mind. Might be useful to mention Benedict’s name to shake things up. Well, there’s no point in being tense about it now.”

“Shall we take a break then?”

“Sounds good.”

“I’ll help.”

As the conversation reached a natural stopping point, Grace worked together with Ashley to prepare cold tea. They poured it into wooden cups and passed them around to everyone.

“I also brought some baked sweets. There’s enough for the others too.”

“Understood. Elmer-san, could I have a moment?”

Leaning out the dragon palanquin window to call to the adjacent palanquin, Elmer appeared at the other window.

“What is it?”

“I’m sending over a canteen of tea and some baked sweets. Please share them.”

Using Levitation, I sent a canteen filled with tea and a box packed with baked sweets to the neighboring palanquin.

“This is… thank you. We’ll gratefully accept them.”

Elmer smiled as he received them.

Suddenly, when I turned around, my eyes met Sheila’s. In her hand, a deck of cards was shining brilliantly.

“Cards, play?”

Princess Stephania and the Zilbolt marquis household members tilted their heads in confusion.

Ah. That might be good too. There are some inexperienced players. Alfred and Viola also seemed to be taking a break from their work, so the timing might be just right.

+++

# **245 – Marquisate of Fobrestar**

Our journey continued with the group divided into beginners and experienced players, enjoying card games along the way.

With so many people – including Princess Stephania, Tephra, and the members of the Zilbolt household who had never played cards before – we had prepared multiple sets so everyone could play separately.

Since I needed to explain the rules, I decided to join the beginners’ group and play while teaching.

“Father, I’m sorry. I’m going out with this.”

“Hmm. It seems Romina has bested me this time.”

Marquis Zilbolt, who had drawn the joker from Romina’s hand and lost by a narrow margin, nonetheless narrowed his eyes happily.

“There are so many ways to play this. Perhaps I should buy some when we return to Termwills…”

“Human games are quite complex, but fascinating.”

“No, Theodore-dono’s game is quite innovative – there’s nothing else like it.”

It seemed everyone had taken a liking to it, which was a relief.

Just then, Lavigne let out a small bark.

“My, how clever, Marlene.”

The experienced group seemed to be having fun too. Rosemary smiled.

They appeared to be playing Page One. Marlene had raised her hand when she had only one card left, and Lavigne, who was waiting behind Ashley, had barked softly and declared Page One on Marlene’s behalf.

“Thank you, Lavigne.”
